vedāntavākyakusumagrathanārthatvātsūtrāṇām

vākyārthavicāraṇādhyavasānanirvṛttā hi brahmāvagatiḥ nānumānādipramāṇāntaranirvṛttā 
satsu tu vedāntavākyeṣu jagato janmādikāraṇavādiṣu tadarthagrahaṇadādaya anumānamapi vedāntavākyāvirodhi pramāṇaṃ bhavat na nivāryate śrutyaiva ca sahāyatvena tarkasyāpya bhyupetatvāt 
tathā hi  śrotavyo mantavyaḥ' iti śruti 'paṇḍito medhāvī gandhārānevopasaṃpadyetaivamevehācāryavānpuruṣo veda' iti ca puruṣabuddhisāhāyyamātmano darśayati 
na dharmajijñāsāyāmiva śrutyāya evaṃ pramāṇaṃ brahmajijñāsāyām 
kiṃtu śru tyādayo'nubhavādayaśca yathāsaṃbhavamiha pramāṇam anubhavāvasānatvādbhutavastuviṣayatvācca brahmajñānasya 
kartavye hi viṣaye nānubhavāpekṣāstīti śrutyādīnāmeva prāmāṇyaṃ syāt puruṣādhīnātmalābhatvācca kartavyasya 
kartumakartumanyathā vā kartuṃ śakyaṃ laukikaṃ vaidikaṃ ca karma
yathā aśvena gacchati padbhayām anyathā vā na vā gacchatīti 
tathā 'atirātre ṣoḍaśinaṃ gṛhṇāti nātirātre ṣoḍaśinaṃ gṛhṇāti udite juhoti anudite juhoti' iti 
vidhipratiṣedhāśca atra arthavantaḥ sūtrabhāṣye pā syuḥ vikalpotsargāpavādāśca 
na tu vastu 'evam naivam' asti nāsti' iti vā vikalpyate

svaśabdenaiva ceha purastādupariṣṭācca brahma saṃkīrtyate'puruṣa evedaṃ viśvaṃ karma tapo brahma parāmṛtam' iti 'brahmaivedamamṛtaṃ purastādbrahma paścādbrahma dakṣiṇataścottareṇa 'iti ca 
tatra tvāya tanāyatanavadbhāvaśravaṇān 
sarva brahmeti ca sāmānādhikaraṇyāta yathā hyanekātmako vṛkṣa śākhā skandho mūlaṃ ceti evaṃ nānāraso vicitra ātmetyāśaṅkā saṃbhavati 
tāṃ nivartayituṃ sāvadhāraṇamāha 'tamevaikaṃ jānatha ātmāsū prathamo'dhyāyaḥ 
nama' iti 
etaduktaṃ bhavati na kāryaprapañcaviśiṣṭo vicitra ātmā vijñeya 
kiṃ tarhi avidyākṛtaṃ kāryaprapañcaṃ vidyayā pravilāpayanta tamevaikamāyatanabhūtamātmānaṃ jānatha ekarasamiti 
yathā 'yasminnāste devadattastadānaya' ityukte āsanamevānayati na devadattama
tadvadāyatanabhūtasyaivaikarasakhātmano vijñeyatvamupadiśyate 
vikārānṛtābhisaṃdhasya cāpavādaḥ śrūyate 'mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyumāpnoti ya iha nāneva paśyati' iti 
'sarva brahma' iti tu sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ prapañcavilāpanārthama na anekarasatāpratipādanārthama yathā saindhavavano'nantaro'bāhyaḥ kṛtsno rasaghana evaivaṃ vā are'yamātmānantaro'bāhyaḥ kṛtsna prajñānaghana eva' ityekarasatāśravaṇāta 
tasmāibhvādyāyatanaṃ paraṃ brahma 
yattūktamsetuśruteḥ setośca pāravattvopapatte brahmaṇo'rthāntareṇa yubhavādyāyatanena bhavitavyamiti atrocyatevidhāraṇatvamātrameva setuśrutyā vivakṣyate na pāravattvādi 
na hi mṛhārumayo loke seturdṛṣṭa ityatrāpi mṛdārumaya eva seturabhyupagamyate 
setuśabdārtho'pi vidhāraṇatvamātrameva na pāravattvādi ṣiño bandhanakarmaṇa setuśavdavyutpatteḥ 
apara āha 'tamevaikaṃ jānatha ātmānama' iti yadetatsaṃkīsūtrabhāṣye pā rtitamātmajñānam yaccaitat 'anyā vāco vimuñcatha' iti vāgvimocanam tat atra amṛtatvasādhanatvāt 'amṛtasyaiṣa setu 'iti setuśrutyā saṃkīrtyate
na tu yubhvādyāyatanam 
tatra yaduktam setuśruterbrahmaṇo'rthāntareṇa dyubhvādyāyatanena bhavitavyamiti etadayuktam 
muktopasṛpyavyapadeśāt 
itaśca parameva brahma bhvādyāyatanam 
yasmānmuktopasṛpyatāsya vyapadiśyamānā dṛśyate 
muktairupasṛpyaṃ muktopasṛpyam 
dehādiṣvanātmasu ahamasmītyātmabuddhiravidyā tatastatpūjanādau rāgaḥ tatparibhavādau ca dveṣa taducchedadarśanādbhayaṃ mohaśca ityevamayamanantabhedo'narthavrāta saṃtata sarveṣāṃ naḥ pratyakṣaḥ 
tadviparyayeṇāvidyārāgadveṣādidoṣamuktairupasṛpyamupagamyametaditi dyubhvādyāyatanaṃ prakṛtya vyapadeśo bhavati 
katham  'bhidyate hṛdayagranthiśchidyante sarvasaṃśayā 
śrīyante cāsya karmāṇi tasmindṛṣṭe parāvare' ityuktvā bravīti 'tathā vidvānnāmarūpādvimuktaḥ parātparaṃ puruṣamupaiti divyama' iti 
brahmaṇaśca muktopasṛpyatvaṃ prasiddhaṃ śāstre 'yadā sarve pramucyante kāmā ye'sya hṛdi śritāḥ 
atha martyo'mṛto bha vatyatra brahma samaśnute' ityevamādau 
pradhānādīnāṃ tu nakkasū prathamo'dhyāyaḥ 
cinmuktopasṛpyatvamasti prasiddham 
api ca 'tamevaikaṃ jānatha ātmānamanyā vāco vimuñcathāmṛtasyaiṣa setuḥ' iti vāgvimokapūrvakaṃ vijñeyatvamiha yubhvādyāyatanasyocyate 
taca śrutyantare brahmaṇo dṛṣṭam 'tameva dhīro vijñāya prajñāṃ kurvīta brāhmaṇa 
nānudhyāyāvahūñ śabdānvāco viglāpanaṃ hi tat' iti 
tasmādapi bhvādyāyatanaṃ paraṃ brahma 
nānumānamatacchandāt 
yathā brahmaṇa pratipādako vaiśeṣiko heturuktaḥ naivamarthāntarasya vaiśeṣiko hetu pratipādako'stītyāha 
nānumānaṃ sāṃkhyasmṛtiparikalpitaṃ pradhānam iha yubhvādyāyatanatvena pratipattavyam 
kasmāt  atacchabdāt 
tasyācetanasya pradhānasya pratipādakaḥ śabdaḥ tacchabdaḥ na tacchabdaḥ atacchabdaḥ 
na hyatrācetanasya pradhānasya pratipādakaḥ kaścicchabdo'sti yenācetanaṃ pradhānaṃ kāraṇatvenāyatanatvena vāvagamyeta 
tadvipa rītasya cetanasya pratipādakaśabdo'trāsti 'yaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvavit' ityādiḥ 
ata eva na vāyurapīha yubhvādyāyatanatvena 
prāṇabhṛcca 
yadyapi prāṇabhṛto vijñānātmana ātmatvaṃ cetanatvaṃ ca saṃ sūtrabhāṣye pā bhavati tathāpyupādhiparicchinnajñānasya sarvajñatvādyasaṃbhave sati asmādevātacchadāt prāṇabhūpi na yubhvādyāyatanatvenāśrayitavyaḥ 
na copādhiparicchinnasyāvibhoḥ prāṇabhṛto yubhvādyāyatanatvamapi samyaksaṃbhavati 
pṛthagyogakaraṇamuttarārtham 
ENSING kutaśca na prāṇabhṛt bhvādyāyatanatvenāśrayitavya bhedavyapadeśāt 
bhedavyapadeśaceha bhavati  'tamevaikaṃ jānatha ātmānam 'iti jñeyajñātṛbhāvena 
tatra prāṇabhṛta tāvanmumukṣutvājjñātā 
pariśeṣādātmaśabdavācyaṃ brahma jñeyaṃ śubhvādyāyatanamiti gamyate na prāṇabhṛt 
kutaśca na prāṇabhṛt dyubhvādyāyatanatvenāśrayitavyaḥ prakaraṇāt 
prakaraṇaṃ cedaṃ paramātmanaḥ kasminnu bhagavo vijñāte sarvamidaṃ vijñātaṃ bhavati' ityekavijñānena sarvavijñānāpekṣaṇāt 
paramātmani hi sarvātmake vijñāte sarvamidaṃ vijñātaṃ syāt na kevale prāṇabhṛti 
kutaśca na prāṇabhṛt bhvādyāyatanatvenāśrayitavyaḥ prathamo'dhyāyaḥ 
sthityadanābhyāṃ ca 
na yubhavādyāyatanaṃ ca prakṛtya 'dvā suparṇā sayujā sakhāyā' ityatra sthityadane nirdiśyate
'tayoranyaḥ pippalaṃ svādvatti' iti karmaphalāśanam 
'anaśnannanyo'bhicākaśīti' ityaudāsīnye nāvasthānam 
tābhyāṃ ca sthityadnābhyāmīśvarakṣetrajñau tatra gṛhyete 
yadi ca īśvaro bhvādyāyatanatvena vivakṣitaḥ tatastasya prakṛtasyeśvarasya kṣetrajñātpṛthagvacanamavakalpate 
anyathā hyaprakṛtavacanamākasmikamasaṃbaddhaṃ syāt 
nanu tavāpi kṣetrajñasyeśvarātpṛthagvacanamākasmikameva prasajyeta
na tasyāvivakṣitatvāt 
kṣetrajño hi kartṛtvena bhoktṛtvena ca pratiśarīraṃ buddhayādhupādhisaṃbaddha lokata eva prasiddha nāsau śrutyā tātparyeṇa vivakṣyate
īśvarastu lokato'prasiddhatvācchrutyā tātparyeṇa vikṣyati na tasyākasmikaṃ vacanaṃ yuktam 
'guhāṃ praviṣṭāvātmānau hi 'ityatrāpyetaddarśitam 'dvā suparṇā' ityasyāmṛci īśvarakṣetrajñāyete iti 
yadāpi paiṅgayupaniṣatkṛtena vyākhyānenāsyāmṛci sattvakṣetrajñāvucyete tadāpi na virodha kaścit 
katham  prāṇabhṛddhīha ghaṭādicchidravat sattvāyupādhyabhimānitvena pratiśarīraṃ gṛhyamāṇo bhvādyāyatanaṃ na bhavatīti sū sūtrabhāṣye pā pratiṣidhyate 
yastu sarvaśarīreṣūpādhibhirvinopalakṣyate paraeva sa bhavati
yathā ghaṭādicchidrāṇi ghaṭādibhirupādhibhivinopalakṣyamāṇāni mahākāśa eva bhavanti tadvat prāṇabhṛtaḥ parasmādanyatvānupapatteḥ pratiṣedho nopapadyate 
tasmātmattvāyupādhyabhimānina eva bhvādyāyatanatvapratiṣedhaḥ 
tasmātparameva brahma yubhvādyāyatanam 
tadetat 'adṛśyatvādiguṇako dharmokteḥ' ityanenaiva siddham 
tasyaiva hi bhūtayonivākyasya madhye idaṃ paṭhitam 'yasmindyauḥ pṛthivī cāntarikṣam' iti 
prapañcārthaṃ tu punarupanyastam 
bhūmā saṃprasādādadhyupadeśāt 
karaṇam 
idaṃ samāmananti 'bhūmā tveva vijijñāsitavya iti bhūmānaṃ bhagavo vijijñāsa iti 
yatra nānyatpaśyati bhūmādhi nānyacchṛṇoti nānyadvijānāti sa bhūmā 
atha yatrānyatpaśyatyanyacchṛṇotyanyadvijānāti tadalpam' ityādi 
tatra saṃśayaḥ kiṃ prāṇo bhūmā syāt āhosvitparamātmeti 
kuta saṃśaya  bhūmeti tāvadvaddutvamabhidhīyate
'baholopo bhū ca baho 'iti bhūmaśabdasya bhāvapratyayāntatāsmaraṇāt 
kimātmakaṃ punastadvahutvamiti viśeṣākāṅkṣāyām 'prāṇo vā āśāyā bhūyān' iti sū prathamo'dhyāyaḥ 
saṃnidhānāt prāṇo bhūmeti pratibhāti 
tathā 'śrutaṃ hyeva me bhagavaddṛśebhyastarati śokamātmaviditi 
so'haṃ bhagavaḥ śocāmi taṃ mā bhagavāñśokasya pāraṃ tārayatu 'iti prakaraṇotthānātparamātmā bhūmetyapi pratibhāti 
tatra kasyopādānaṃ nyāyyam kasya vā hānamiti bhavati saṃśaya 
kiṃ tāvatprāptam  prāṇo bhūmeti 
kasmāt  bhūyaḥpraśnaprativacanaparaṃparādarśanāt 
yathā hi 'asti bhagavo nāmno bhūya 'iti 'vāgvāva nāmno bhūyasī' iti 
tathā 'asti bhagavo vāco bhūya 'iti 'mano vāva vāco bhūyaḥ' iti ca nāmādibhyo hi ā prāṇāt bhūyaḥ praśnaprativacanapravāha pravṛttaḥ 
naivaṃ prāṇātparaṃ bhūyaḥ praśna prativacanaṃ dṛśyateasti bhagava prāṇādbhūya 'iti 'ado vāva prāṇāyaḥ' iti 
prāṇameva tu nāmādibhya āśāntebhyo bhūyāṃsam 'prāṇo vā āśāyā bhūyān' ityādinā saprapañcamuktvā prāṇadarśinaścātivāditvam 'ativādyasītyativādyasmīti brūyānnāpahnu vīta' ityabhyanujñāya 'eṣa tu vā ativadati yaḥ satyenātivadati' iti prāṇavratamativāditvamanukṛṣya aparityajyaiva prāṇaṃ satyādiparaṃparayā bhūmānamavatārayan prāṇameva bhūmānaṃ manyata iti gamyate 
kathaṃ punaḥ prāṇe bhūmani vyākhyāyamāne 'yatrasūkhabhāpye pā nānyatpaśyati' ityetadbhūmno lakṣaṇaparaṃ vacanaṃ vyākhyāyeteti ucyatesuṣuptāvasthāyāṃ prāṇagrasteṣu karaṇeṣu darśanādivyavahāranivṛttidarśanātsaṃbhavati prāṇasyāpi 'yatra nānyatpaśyatīti' etallakṣaṇam 
tathā ca śrutiḥ 'na śṛṇoti na paśyati' ityādinā sarvakaraṇavyāpārapratyastamayarūpāṃ suṣuptyavasthāmuktvā prāṇāmaya evaitasminpure jāgrati' iti tasyāmevāvasthāyāṃ pañcavṛtte prāṇasya jāgaraṇaṃ bruvatī prāṇapradhānāṃ suṣuptyavasthāṃ darśayati 
yaccaitadbhūmnaḥ sukhatvaṃ śrutam'yo vai bhūmā tatsukham 'iti tadpyaviruddham 
'atraiṣa deva svapnānna paśyatyatha yadetasmiñśarīre sukhaṃ bhavati' iti suṣuptyavasthāyāmeva sukhaśravaṇāt 
yacca 'yo vai bhūmā tadamṛtama' iti tadapi prāṇasyāviruddhama
'prāṇo vā amṛtam' iti śruteḥ 
kathaṃ punaḥ prāṇaṃ bhūmānaṃ manyamānasya 'tarati śokamātmavit' ityātmavividiṣayā prakaraṇasyotthānamupapadyate  prāṇa evehātmā vivakṣita iti brūmaḥ 
tathāhi  'prāṇo ha pitā prāṇo mātā prāṇo bhrātā prāṇaḥ svasā prāṇa ācārya prāṇo brāhmaṇa 'iti prāṇameva sarvātmānaṃ karoti 'yathā vā arā nābhau samarpitā evamasminprāṇe sarva samarpitam' iti ca 
sarvātmatvāranābhinidarśanābhyāṃ ca saṃbhasū prathamo'dhyāyaḥ 
vati vaipulyātmikā bhūmarūpatā prāṇasya 
tasmātprāṇo bhūmetyevaṃ prāptam 
tata idamucyate paramātmaiveha bhūmā bhavitumarhati na prāṇa 
kasmāt  saṃprasādādadhyupadeśāt 
saṃprasāda iti suṣuptaṃ sthānamucyate
samyakprasīdatyasminniti nirvacanāt bṛhadāraṇyake ca svapnajāgaritasthānābhyāṃ saha pāṭhāta 
tasyāṃ ca saṃprasādāvasthāyāṃ prāṇo jāgartīti prāṇo'tra saṃprasādo'bhipreyate 
prāṇādūrdhvaṃ bhūna upadiśyamānatvādityarthaḥ 
prāṇa eva cedbhūmā syāt sa eva tasmādūrdhvamupadiśyetetyāśliṣṭametatsyāt 
na hi nāmaiva 'nāmno bhūya 'iti nāmna ūrdhvamupadiG ṭram
kiṃ tarhi nāmno'nyadarthāntaramupadiṣṭaṃ vāgākhyam 'vāgvāva nāmno bhūyasī' iti 
tathā vāgādibhyo'pi ā prāṇādarthāntarameva tatra tatrordhvamupadiṣṭam 
tadvatprāṇādūrdhvamupadiśyamāno bhūmā prāṇādarthāntarabhūto bhavitumarhati 
nanviha nāsti praśna 'asti bhagava prāṇādbhūyaḥ' iti 
nāpi prativacanamasti 'prāṇādvāva bhūyo'sti' iti
kathaṃ prāṇādadhi bhūmopadiśyata ityucyate  prāṇaviṣayameva cātivāditvamuttaratvānukṛṣyamāṇaṃ paśyāma 'eṣa tu vā ativadati yaḥ satyenātivadati' iti 
tasmānnāsti prāṇādadhyupadeśa iti sūtrabhāṣye JA avocyate na tāvatprāṇaviṣayasyaivātivāditvasyaitadanukarṣaṇamiti śakyaṃ vaktuma viśeṣavādāt 'yaḥ satyenātivadati iti 
nanu viśeṣavādo'pyayaṃ prāṇaviṣaya eva bhaviṣyati

kena tarhi  agnihotreṇaiva

tathā 'eṣa tu vā ativadati yaḥ satyenātivadati 'ityukte na satyavadanenātivāditvam 
kena tarhi  prakṛtena prāṇavijñānenaiva 
satyavadanaṃ tu prāṇavido viśeṣo vivakṣyata iti neti brūmaḥ
śrutyarthaparityāgaprasaṅgāt

'satyaṃ tveva vijijñāsitavyam' iti ca prayatnāntarakaraṇamarthāntaravivakṣāṃ sūcayati

tatra prāṇāntamanuśāsanaṃ śrutvā tūṣṇīṃbhūtaṃ nāradaṃ svayameva sanatkumāro vyutpādayati yatprāṇavijñānena vikārānṛtaviṣayeṇātivāditvamanativāditvameva tat eṣa tu vā ativadati yaḥ satyenātivadati' iti

'satyaṃ jñānamanantaṃ brahma' iti ca śrutyantarāt 
tathā vyutpātitāya nāradāya 'so'haṃ bhagavaḥ satyenātivadāni ityevaṃ pravṛttāya vijñānādisādhanaparaṃparayā bhūmānamupadiśati 
tatra yatprāṇādadhi satyaṃ vaktavyaṃ pratijñātam tadeveha bhūmetyucyata iti gamyate

evaṃ cehātmavividiṣayā prakaraṇasyotthānamupapannaṃ bhavidhyati 
prāṇa evehātmā vivakṣita ityetadapi nopapadyate 
na hi prāṇasya mukhyayā vṛttyātmatvamasti

api ca ye bhūniyante dharmā te paramātmanyupapayatna nānyatpaśyati nānyacchṛṇoti nānyadvijānāti sa bhūmā' iti darśanādivyavahārābhāvaṃ bhūmani avagamayati 
paramātmani cāyaṃ darśanādivyavahārābhāvo'vagataḥ 'yatra tvasya sarvamātmaivābhūttatkena kaṃ paśyet' ityādiśrutyantarāt 
yo'pyasau suṣupyavasthāyāṃ darśanādivyavahārābhāva ukta so'pyātmana evāsaṅgatvavivakṣayoktaḥ na prāṇasvabhāvavivaśyā paramātmaprakaraṇāt 
yadapi tasyāmavasthāyāṃ sukhamuktama tadapyātmana eva sukharūpatvavivakṣayoktama

ihāpi 'yo vai bhūmā tatsukhaṃ nālpe sukhamasti bhūmaiva sukham sū prathamo'dhyāyaḥ 
iti sāmayasukhanirākaraṇena brahmaiva sukhaṃ bhūmānaṃ darśayati

tadeva cāsya pāramārthikaṃ svarūpama yena śarīrātsamutthāya svena rūpeṇābhiniṣpadyate 
kathaṃ punaḥ svaṃ ca rūpaṃ svenaiva ca niṣpadyata iti saṃbhavati kūṭasthanityasya  suvarṇādīnāṃ tu dravyāntarasaṃparkādabhibhūtasvarūpāṇāmanabhivyaktāsādhāraṇaviśeṣāṇāṃ kṣāraprakṣepādibhiḥ śodhyamānānāṃ svarūpeṇābhiniṣpatti syātū

yathā śuddhasya sphaṭikasya svācchayaṃ śauklyaṃ ca svarūpaṃ prāgvivekagrahaṇādraktanīlādyapādhibhiraviviktamiva bhavati

padiśati 
yo'kṣiṇi prasiddhodraṣṭā draṣṭṛtvena vibhāvyate so'mṛtābhayalakṣaṇādbrahmaṇo'nyaścetsyān tato'mṛtābhayabrahmasāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ na syāt 
nāpi praticchāyātmāyamakṣilakṣito nirdiśyate prajāpatermṛṣāvāditvaprasaṅgān 
tathā dvitīye'pi paryāye 'ya eṣa svapne mahīyamānaścarati' iti na prathamaparyāya nirdiṣṭādakṣipuruṣāddūṣṭuranyo nirdiṣṭa 'etaṃ tveva te bhūyo'nuvyākhyāsyāmi' ityupakramāt 
kiṃca 'ahamadya svapne hastinamadrākṣama nedānī taṃ paśyāmi' iti dṛṣṭameva pratibuddha pratyācaṣṭe 
draṣṭāraṃ tu tameva pratyabhijānāti  'ya evāhaṃ svapnamadrākṣam sa evāhaṃ jāgaritaṃ paśyāmi 'iti 
tathā tṛtīye'pi paryāyenāha khalvayamevaṃ saṃpratyātmānaṃ jānātyayamahmasmīti no evemāni bhūtāni' iti suṣuptāvasthāyāṃ viśeṣavijñānābhāvameva darśayati na vijñātāraṃ pratiṣedhati 
yattu tatra 'vināśamevāpīto bhavati iti tadapi viśeṣavijñānavināśābhiprāyameva na vijñātṛvināśābhiprāyama
'na hi vijñāturvijñāterviparilopo vidyate'vināśitvāt 'iti śrutyantarāt 
tathā caturthe'pi paryāye 'etaṃ tveva te bhūyo'nuvyākhyāsyāmi no evānyatraitaṃsmāt' ityupakramya 'maghavan martya vā idaṃ śarīrama' ityāS W  sūtrabhāṣye pā dinā prapañcena śarīrādyapādhisaṃbandhapratyākhyānena saṃprasādaśadoditaṃ jīvama 'svena rūpeṇābhiniṣpadyate' iti brahmasvarūpāpa darśayana na parasmādbrahmaṇo'mṛtābhayasvarūpādanyaṃ jīvaṃ darśayati 
kecittu paramātmavivakṣāyāma 'etaṃ tveva te' iti jīvākarṣaṇamanyāyyaṃ manyamānā etameva vākyopakramasūcitamapahtapāpmatvādiguṇakamātmānaṃ taṃ bhūyo'nuvyākhyāmyāmīni kalpayanti

tammāt yadavidyāpratyupasthāpitamapāramārthika jaivaṃ rūpaṃ kartṛtvabhoktṛtvarāgadveṣādidoṣakaluṣitamanekānarthayogi tadvilayanena tadviparītamapahatapāpmatvādiguṇakaṃ pārameśvara svarūpaṃ vidyayā pratipadyate sarpādivilayaneneva rajjvādīna 
apare tu vādinaḥ pāramārthikameva jaivaṃ rūpamiti manyante'smadīyāśca kecit 
teṣāṃ sarveṣāmātyaikatva samyagdarśanapratipakṣabhūtānāṃ pratiṣedhāyedaṃ śārīrakamārabdhama eka eva parameśvara kūṭasthanityo vijñānadhāturavidyayā māyayā māyāvivat anekadhā vibhāvyate nāsū prathamo'dhyāyaḥ 
nyo vijñānadhāturastīti 
yattvidaṃ parameśvaravākye jīvamāśaṅkaya pratiṣedhati sūlakāra 'nāsaṃbhavāt' ityādinā tatrāyamabhiprāya nityaśuddhabuddhamuktasvabhāve kūṭastha nitye ekasminnasaṅge paramātmani tadviparītaṃ jaivaṃ rūpaṃ vyomnīva talamalādi parikalpitam 
tat ātmaikatvapratipādanaparairvākyainyayopetaidvaitavāda pratiṣedhaiścāpaneṣyāmīti paramātmano jīvādanyatvaṃ draḍhayati

kiṃ tvanuvadatyevāvidyākalpitaṃ lokaprasiddhaṃ jīvabhedam

NANDA anyārthaśca parāmarśaḥ 
atha yo'yaṃ daharavākyaśeṣe jīvaparāmarśo darśitaḥ ya eṣa saṃprasāda 'ityādiḥ sa dahare parameśvare vyākhyāyamāne na jīvopāsanopadeśaḥ nāpi prakṛtaviśeṣopadeśaḥ ityanarthakatvaṃ prāpnotītyata āha anyārtho'yaṃ jīvaparāmarśo na jīvasvarūpaparyavasāyī
kiṃ tarhi parameśvarasvarūpaparyavasā athasūtrabhāṣye yī 
katham  saṃprasādaśabdodito jīvo jāgaritavyavahāre dehendriyapañjarādhyakṣo bhūtvā tadvāsanānirmitāṃśca svapnānnāḍīcaro'nubhūya śrāntaḥ śaraṇaṃ prepsurubhayarūpādapi śarīrābhimānātsamutthāya suṣuptāvasthāyāṃ paraṃ jyotirākāśaśabditaṃ paraṃ brahmopasaṃpadya viśeṣavijñānavattvaṃ ca parityajya svena rūpeṇābhiniṣpadyate
yadasyopasaṃpattavyaṃ paraṃ jyotiḥ yena svena rūpeṇāyamabhiniṣpadyate sa eṣa ātmāpahtapāpmatvādiguṇa upāsyaḥ ityevamartho'yaṃ jīvaparāmarśa parameśvaravā dino'pyupapadyate

tasya parihāro vaktavya 
ukto hyasya parihāra parameśvare'pyāpekṣika malpatvamavakalpata iti 'arbhakaukastvāttavyapadeśāca neti cenna nicāyyatvādevaṃ vyomavacca' ityatra 
sa eveha parihāro'nusaṃdhātavya iti sūca yati

anukṛtestasya ca 
anukṛtya'na tatra sūryo bhāti na candratārakaṃ nemā vidyuto bhānti kuto'yamagniḥ 
tameva bhāntamanubhāti sarva tasya bhāsā sarvamidaṃ vibhāti' iti samāmananti 
dhikaraṇam 
tatra yaṃ bhāntamanubhāti sarve yasya ca bhāsā sarvamidaṃ vibhāti sa kiṃ tejodhātuḥ kaścit uta prājña ātmeti vicikitsāyāṃ tejodhāturiti tāvatprāptam 
kutaḥ  tejodhātūnāmeva sūryādīnāṃ bhānapratiṣedhāt 
tejasvabhāvakaṃ hi candratārakādi teja svabhāvaka eva sūrye bhāsamāne ahani na bhāsata iti prasiddham 
tathā saha sūryeṇa sarvamidaṃ candratārakādi yasminna bhāsate so'pi teja svabhāva eva kaści dityavagamyate

anukaraṇamanukṛti

tu tejodhātuṃ kaṃcitsūryādayo'nubhāntīti prasiddham 
sūtrabhāṣye pā samatvāñca tejodhātūnāṃ sūryādīnāṃ na tejodhātumanyaṃ pratyapekṣāsti yaṃ bhāntamanubhāyu
na hi pradīpa pradīpāntaramanubhāti

'anukṛte 'ityanubhānamasusūcat
'tasya ca 'iti caturtha pādamasya lokasya sūcayati

taddevā jyotiṣāṃ jyotirāyurhopāsate'mṛtam' iti hi prājñamātmānamāmananti 
tejontareṇa tu sūryāditejo vibhātītyaprasiddhama viruddhaṃ ca
tejontareṇa tejontarasya pratighātāt 
athavā na sūryādīnāmeva ślokaparipaṭhitānāmidaṃ taddhetukaṃ vibhānamucyate
kiṃ tarhi 'sarvamidama' ityaviśeṣaśruteḥ sarvasyaivāsya nāmarūpakriyākārakaphalajātasya yā abhivyaktiḥ sā brahmajyoti sattānimittā
yathā sūryajyoti sattānimittā sarvasya rūpajātasyābhivyaktiḥ tadvat 
' na tatra sūryo bhāti' iti ca tatra śabdamāharanprakṛtagrahaṇaṃ darśayati
prakṛtaṃ ca brahma 'yasmindyauḥ pṛthivī cāntarikṣamotama' ityāsū prathamo'dhyāyaḥ 
dinā
anantaraṃ ca 'hiraṇmaye pare kośe virajaṃ brahma nikalama 
tacchubhraṃ jyotiṣāṃ jyotistadyadātmavido viduḥ' iti

tatra tu sa eva tejodhāturanyo na saṃbhavatītyupapāditam 
brahmaṇyapi caiṣāṃ bhānapratiṣedho'vakalpate
yataḥ yadupalabhyate tatsarvaṃ brahmaṇaiva jyotiṣopalabhyate
brahma tu nānyena jyotiṣopalabhyate svayaṃ jyoti svarūpatvāta yena sūryādaya mtasminbhāyuḥ 
brahma hi anyadvayanakti na tu brahmānyena vyajyate 'ātmanaivāyaṃ jyotiṣāste agṛhyo na hi gṛhyate' ityādiśrutibhyaḥ

na hyanantāyāmavistārasya paramātmano'ṅguṣṭaparimāṇatvamupapadyate
vijñānātmanastūpādhimattvātsaṃbhavati kayācitkalpanayāṅguṣṭamātratvama

aṅguṣṭhamātraṃ puruṣaṃ niścakarṣa yamo balāt' iti na hi parameśvaro balāt yamena niṣkraṣṭuṃ śakyaḥ
tena tatra saṃsārī aṅguṣṭhamātro niścita 
sa evehāpītyevaṃ prāpte śramaḥ paramātmaivāyamaṅguṣṭhamātraparimitaḥ puruṣo bhavituma rhati

tathā ca brāhmaṇam 'anena jīvenātmanānupraviśya nāmarūpe vyākaravāṇi 'ityevaṃjātīyakaṃ parasyaivātmano jīvabhāvenāvasthānaṃ darśayati
mantravarṇaśca sarvāṇi rūpāṇi vicitya dhīro nāmāni kṛtvābhivadanyadāste' ityevaṃjātīyakaḥ 
na ca tejaḥ prabhṛtīnāṃ sṛṣṭau jīvasya pṛthaksṛṣṭi śrutā yena parasmādātmano'nyastadvikāro jīvaḥ syāt 
kāśakṛtsnasyācāryasyāvikṛtaḥ parameśvaro jīvaḥ nānya iti matama
āśmarathyasya tu yadyapi jīvasya parasmādananyatvamabhipretam tathāpi 'pratijñāsiddheḥ' iti sāpekṣatvābhidhānātkāryakāraṇabhāva kiyānapyabhipreta iti gamyate
auḍḍulomipakṣe punaḥ spaṣṭamevāvasthāntarāpekṣau bhedābhedau gamyete 
tatra kāśakṛtstrīyaṃ mataṃ śrutyanusārīti gamyate pratipipāda yiṣitārthānusārāt 'tattvamasi' ityādiśrutibhyaḥ
evaṃ ca nsū prathamo'dhyāyaḥ 
sati tajjñānādamṛtatvamavakalpate
vikārātmakatve hi jīvasyābhyupagamyamāne vikārasya prakṛtisaṃbandhe pralayaprasaṅgānna tajjñānādamṛtatvamavakalpeta 
ataśca svāśrayasya nāmarūpasyāsaṃbhavādupādhyāśrayaṃ nāmarūpaṃ jīve upacaryate 
ata evotpattirapi jīvasya kvacidagnivisphuliṅgodāharaṇena śrāvyamāṇā upādhyāyaiva veditavyā 
yadapyuktaṃ prakṛtasyaiva mahato bhūtasya draṣṭavyasya bhūtebhya samutthānaṃ vijñānātmabhāvena darśayanvijñānātmana evedaṃ draṣṭavyatvaṃ darśayatīti tatrāpīyameva trisūtrī yojayitavyā 
'pratijñāsiddherliṅgamāśmarathyaḥ' idamatra pratijñātam 'ā tmani vidite sarvamidaṃ viditaṃ bhavati' 'idaṃ sarve yadayamātmā' iti ca 
upapāditaṃ ca sarvasya nāmarūpakarmaprapañcasyaikaprasavatvādekapralayatvācca dundubhyādidṛṣṭāntaiśca kāryakāraṇayoravyatirekapratipādanāt
tasyā eva pratijñāyā siddhiṃ sūcayatyetalliṅgam yanmahato bhūtasya bhūtebhyaḥ samutthānaṃ vijñānātmabhāvena kathitama ityāśmarathya ācāryo manyate abhede hi satyeka vijñānena sarvavijñānaṃ pratijñātamavakalpata iti 
utkramiṣyata evaṃbhāvādityauḍulomi 'utkramiṣyato vijñānātmano jñānadhyānādisāmarthyātsaṃprasannasya pareṇātmanaikyasūtrabhāṣye pā MA saṃbhavādidamabhedābhidhānamityauḍulomirācāryo manyate 
'ava sthiteriti kāśakṛtstraḥ' asyaiva paramātmano'nenāpi vijñānātmabhāvenāvasthānādupapannamidamabhedābhidhānamiti kāśakṛtsna ācāryo manyate 
nanūcchedābhidhānametat 'etebhyo bhūtebhya samutthāya tānyevānuvinaśyati na pretya saṃjñāsti' iti
kathametadbhedābhidhānam naiṣa doṣaḥ 
viśeṣavijñānavināśābhiprāyametadvināśābhidhānama nātmocchedābhiprāyam
atraiva mā bhagavānamūmuhanna pretya saṃjñāsti' iti paryanuyujya svayameva śrutyā arthāntarasya darśitatvāt 'na vā are'haṃ mohaṃ bravīmyavināśī vā are'yamātmānucchittidharmā mātrāsaṃsargastvasya bhavati' iti 
etaduktaṃ bhavati kūṭastha nitya evāyaṃ vijñānaghana ātmā
nāsyocchedaprasaṅgo'sti
mātrābhistvasya bhūtendriyalakṣaṇābhiravidyākṛtābhirasaṃsargo vi dyayā bhavati
saṃsargābhāve ca tatkṛtasya viśeṣavijñānasyābhāvāt 'na pretya saṃjñāsti' ityuktamiti 
yadapyuktam'vi jñātāramare kena vijānīyāt' iti kartṛvacanena śabdenopasaṃhārādvijñānātmana evedaṃ draṣṭavyamiti tadapi kāśakṛtstrīyenaiva darśanena pariharaṇīyam 
api ca 'yata hi dvaitamiva bhavati taditara itaraṃ paśyati' ityārabhyāvidyāviṣaye tasyaiva darśaRESsū prathamo'dhyāyaḥ 
nādilakṣaṇaṃ viśeṣavijñānaṃ prapañcaya yatra tvasya sarvamātmai vābhūttatkena kaṃ paśyet' ityādinā vidyāviṣaye tasyaiva darśanādilakṣaṇasya viśeṣavijñānasyābhāvamabhidadhāti
punaśca viṣayābhāve'pyātmānaṃ vijānīyādityāśaṅkaya 'vijñātāra mare kena vijānīyāt' ityāha
tataśca viśeṣavijñānābhāvopapādanaparatvādvākyasya vijñānadhātureva kevala sanbhūtapūrvaṃgatyā kartṛvacanena tṛcā nirdiṣṭa iti gamyate 
darśitaṃ tu purastātkāśakṛtstrīyasya pakṣasya śrutimattvam 
ataśca vijñānātmaparamātmanoravidyāpratyupasthāpita nāma rūparacitadehādyupādhinimitto bhedaḥ na pāramārthika ityeṣo'rthaḥ sarvervedāntavādibhirabhyupagantavyaḥ 'sadeva somyedamapra āsīdekamevādvitīyam' 'ātmaivedaṃ sarvama brahmaivedaṃ sarvam idaṃ sarva yadayamātmā 'nānyo'to'sti draṣṭā 'nānyadato'sti draṣṭṛ' ityevaṃrūpābhyaḥ śrutibhyaḥ
smṛtibhyaśca 'vāsudevaḥ sarvamiti' 'kṣetrajñaṃ cāpi māṃ viddhi sarvakṣetreṣu bhārata 'samaṃ sarveṣu bhūteṣu tiṣṭhantaṃ parameśvaram' ityevarūpābhya 
bhedadarśanāpavādācca 'anyo'sāvanyo'hamasmīti na sa veda yathā paśu' mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyumāpnoti ya iha nāneva paśyati 'ityevaṃjātīyakāt
sa vā eṣa mahānaja ātmājaro'marosūtrabhāṣye pā 'mṛto'bhayo brahma' iti ca ātmani sarvavikriyāpratiṣedhāna
anyathā ca mumukṣūṇāṃ nirapavādavijñānānupapatte suniścitārthatvānupapatteśca 
nirapavādaṃ hi vijñānaṃ sarvākāṅkṣānivartakamātmaviṣayamiṣyate'vedāntavijñānasuniścitārthāḥ' iti ca śruteḥ 
tatra ko mohaḥ kaḥ śoka ekatvamanupaśyataḥ' iti ca
sthitaprajñalakṣaṇasmṛteśca 
sthite ca kṣetrajñaparamātmaikatvaviṣaye samyagdarśane kṣetrajñaḥ paramātmeti nāmamātrabhedātkṣetrajño'yaṃ paramātmano bhinnaḥ paramātmāyaṃ kṣetrajñādbhinna ityevaṃjātīyaka ātmabhedaviṣayo'yaṃ nirbandho nirarthakaeko hyayamātmā nāmamātrabhedena bahudhābhidhīyata iti 
na hi 'satyaṃ jñānamanantaṃ brahma 
yo veda nihitaṃ guhāyām' iti kāṃcidevaikāṃ guhāmadhikṛtyaitaduktam 
na ca brahmaṇo'nyo guhāyāṃ nihito'sti 'tatsṛṣṭvā tadevānuprāviśat' iti sraṣṭureva praveśaśravaṇāt 
ye tu nirbandhaṃ kurvanti te vedāntārthaṃ bādhamānā śreyodvāraṃ samyagdarśanameva bādhante 
kṛtakamanityaṃ ca mokṣaṃ kalpayanti
nyāyena ca na saṃgacchanta iti 
prakṛtiśca pratijñādṛṣṭāntānuparodhāt 
yathābhyudayahetutvāddharmo jijñāsya evaṃ niḥśreyasahetutvādbrahmāpi jijñāsyamityuktam 
brahma ca 'janmādyasya yata 'itisū lakṣitama prathamo'dhyāyaḥ 
e prakṛtyadhikaraṇam 

tatra lakṣaṇaṃ ghaṭarucakādīnāṃ mṛtsuvarṇādivatprakṛtitve kulāla suvarṇakārādivannimittatve ca samānamityato bhavati vimarśa kimātmakaṃ punarbrahmaṇa kāraṇatvaṃ syāditi 
tatra nimittakāraṇameva tāvatkevalaṃ syāditi pratibhāti
kasmāta  īkṣāpūrvaNGA kakartṛtvaśravaṇāta īkṣāpūrvakaṃ hi brahmaṇaḥ kartṛtvamavagamyate'sa īkṣāṃcaṝ' 'sa prāṇamasṛjata 'ityādiśrutibhyaḥ
īkṣāpūrvakaṃ ca kartṛtvaṃ nimittakāraṇeṣveva kulālādiṣu dṛṣṭam
anekakārakapūrvikā ca kriyāphalasiddhiloṃke dṛṣṭā 
saca nyāya ādikartaryapi yuktaḥ saṃkramayituma 
īśvaratvaprasiddheśca īśvarāṇāṃ hi rājavaivasvatādīnāṃ nimittakāraṇatvameva kevalaṃ pratīyate
tadvatparameśvarasyāpi nimittakāraṇatvameva yuktaṃ pratipattama 
kārya cedaṃ jagatsāvayavamacetanamaśuddhaṃ ca dṛśyate kāraṇenāpi tasya tādṛśenaiva bhavitavyama kāryakāraṇayo sārūpyadarśanāta
brahma cānevaṃlakṣaṇamavagamyate niṣkalaṃ niṣkriya śāntaṃ niravadyaṃ nirañjanam' ityādiśrutibhyaḥ
pāriśeṣyādbrahmaṇo'nyadupādānakāraṇamaśuddhayādiguṇakaṃ smṛtiprasiddhamabhyupagantavyam brahmakāraṇatvaśruternimittatvamātre paryavasānādityevaṃ prāpte sūtrabhāṣye pā brūmaḥ prakṛti copādānakāraṇaṃ ca brahmābhyupagantavyama nimittakāraṇaṃ ca
na kevalaṃ nimittakāraṇameva
kasmāta pratijñādṛṣṭāntānuparodhāt 
evaṃ hi pratijñādṛṣṭāntau śroto nopurudhyete 
pratijñā tāvat 'uta tamādeśamaprāyo yenāśrutaṃ śrutaṃ bhavatyamataṃ matamavijñātaṃ vijñātam' iti
tatra caikena vijñātena sarvamanyadavijñātamapi vijñātaṃ bhavatīti pratīyate
taccopādānakāraṇavijñāne sarvavijñānaṃ saṃbhavati upādānakāraṇāvyatirekātkāryasya
nimittakāraṇāvyatirekantu kāryasya nāsti loke takṣṇaḥ prāsādvyatirekadarśanāta 
dṛṣṭānto'pi 'yathā somyaikena mṛtpiṇḍena sarve mṛnmayaṃ vijñātaṃ syādvācārambhaṇaṃ vikāro nāmadheyaṃ mṛttiketyeva satyama 'ityupādānakāraṇagocara evāmnāyate
tathā 'ekena lohamaṇi nā sarva lohamayaṃ vijñātaṃ syāt' 'ekena nakhanikṛntanena sarva kārṇāyasaṃ vijñātaṃ syāt' iti ca 
tathānyatrāpi kasminnu bhagavo vijñāte sarvamidaṃ vijñātaṃ bhavati' iti pratijñā 
'yathā pṛthivyāmoṣadhayaḥ saṃbhavanti' iti dṛṣṭāntaḥ 
tathā 'ātmani khalvare dṛṣṭe śrute mate vijñāte idaṃ sarva viditam' iti pratijñā 
sa yathā dundubheīnyamānasya na bāhyāñśabdāñśaknuyāgrahaṇāya dundubhemtu sū prathamo'dhyāyaḥ 
grahaṇena dundubhyāghātasya vā śabdo gṛhītaḥ' iti dṛṣṭāntaḥ 
evaṃ yathāsaṃbhavaṃ prativedāntaṃ pratijñādṛṣṭāntau prakṛtitvasādhanau pratyetavyau 
yata itīyamapi pañcamī 'yato vā imāni bhūtāni jāyante' ityatra 'janikartuḥ prakṛti 'iti viśeṣasmaraṇātprakṛtilakṣaṇa evāpādāne draṣṭavyā 
nimittatvaṃ tvadhiṣṭhātrantarābhāvādadhigantavyama
yathā hi loke mṛtsuvarṇādikamupādānakāraṇaṃ kulālasuvarṇakārādīnadhiṣṭhātṛnapekṣya pravartate naivaṃ brahmaṇa upādānakāraṇasya sato'nyo'dhiṣṭhātā pekṣyo'sti prāgutpatte 'ekamevādvitīyam' ityavadhāraṇāt
adhiṣṭhātrantarā bhāvo'pi pratijñādṛṣṭāntānuparodhādevodito veditavyaadhiṣṭhātari hyupādānādanyasminnabhyupagamyamāne punaradhyekavijñānena sarvavijñānasyāsaṃbhavātpratijñādṛṣṭāntoparodha eva syāt 
tasmādadhiṣṭhātrantarābhāvādātmanaḥ kartṛtvamupādānāntarābhāvācca prakṛtitvam 
kutaścātmanaḥ kartṛtvaprakṛtitve  abhidhyopadeśāca 
abhidhyopadeśaścātmanaḥ kartṛtvaprakṛtitve gamayati 'so'kāmayata bahu syāṃ prajāyeya' iti 'tadaikṣata bahu syāṃ prajāyeya'sūtrabhāṣye pā iti ca 
tatrābhidhyānapūrvikāyā svātantryapravṛtteḥ karteti gamyate 
bahu syāmiti pratyagātmaviṣayatvādvahubhavanābhidhyānasya prakṛtirityapi gamyate 
A sākṣācībhyāmnānāt 
prakṛtitvasyāyamabhyuccayaḥ 
itaśca prakṛtirbrahma yatkāraṇaṃ sākṣādbrahmaiva kāraṇamupādāya ubhau prabhavapralayāvāmnāyate' sarvāṇi ha vā imāni bhūtānyākāśādeva samutpadyante 
ākāśaṃ pratyastaṃ yanti' iti 
yaddhi yasmātprabhavati yasmiṃ śra pralīyate tattasyopādānaṃ prasiddham yathā vrīhiyavādīnāṃ pṛthivī 
'sākṣāt' iti ca upādānāntarānupādānaṃ sūcayati 'ākāśādeva' iti 
pratyastamayaśca nopādānādanyatra kāryasya dṛṣṭaḥ 
ātmakṛteḥ pariṇāmāt 
itaśca prakṛtirbrahma yatkāraṇaṃ brahmaprakriyāyāma 'tadātmānaṃ svayamakuruta' ityātmanaḥ karmatvaṃ kartṛtvaṃ ca darśayati ātmānamiti karmatvam svayamakuruteti kartṛtvama
kathaṃ punaḥ pūrvasiddhasya sataḥ kartṛtvena vyavasthitasya kriyamāṇatvaṃ śakyaṃsū prathamo'dhyāyaḥ 
saṃpādayituma  pariṇāmāditi brūmaḥ pūrvasiddho'pi hi sannātmā viśeṣeṇa vikārātmanā pariṇamayāmāsātmānamiti 
vikārātmanā ca pariṇāmo mṛdādyāsu prakṛtiṣūpalabdha 
svayamiti ca viśeṣaṇānnimittāntarānapekṣatvamapi pratīyate 
' pariṇāmāt' iti vā pṛthaksūtram 
tasyaiṣo'rthaḥ itaśca prakṛ tirbrahma yatkāraṇaṃ brahmaṇa eva vikārātmanā ca pariṇāma sāmānādhikaraṇyenānāyate 'sacca vyantrābhavanniruktaṃ cāniruktaṃ ca' ityādineti 
yoniśca hi gīyate 
itaśca prakṛtirbrahma yatkāraṇaṃ brahma yonirityapi paṭhyate vedānteṣu 'kartāramīśaṃ puruṣaṃ brahmayonima' iti 'yadbhūtayoniṃ paripaśyanti dhīrāḥ' iti ca 
yoniśabdaśca prakṛtivacanasamadhigato loke 'pṛthivī yoniroṣadhivanaspatīnāma' iti 
strīyonerapyastyevāvayavadvāreṇa garne pratyupādānakāraṇatvam 
ka citsthānavacano'pi yoniśabdo dṛṣṭa 'yoniṣṭa indra niṣade akāri 'iti 
vākyaśeṣāttvatva prakṛtivacanatā parigṛhyate 'yathorṇanābhi sṛjate gṛhṇate ca' ityevaṃjātīyakāt 
tadevaṃ prakṛtitvaṃ brahmaṇaḥ prasiddhama 
yatpunaridamuktama īkṣāpūrvakaṃ s W sūtrabhāṣye pā kartṛtvaṃ nimittakāraṇeṣveva kulālādiṣu loke dṛṣṭama nopādānevityādi tatpratyucyatena lokavadiha bhavitavyama
na hyayamanumānagamyo'rthaḥ
śabdagamyatvāttvasyārthasya yathāśabdamiha bhavitavyama
śabdaścekṣiturīśvarasya prakṛtitvaṃ pratipādayatītyavāṃcāma 
punaścaitama vintareṇa prativakṣyāma 
etena sarve vyākhyātā vyā khyātāḥ 
īśna ternāśabdama' ityārabhya pradhānakāraṇavāda sūtraireva puna punarāśaṅkaya nirākṛtaḥ tasya hi pakṣasyopolakāni sarvavyākhyānā kānicilliṅgābhāsāni vedānteṣvāpātena madhikaraṇam 
ndamatīnprati bhāntīti
sa ca kāryakāraṇānanyatvābhyupagamātpratyāsatro vedāntavādasya devalaprabhṛtibhiśca kaiściddharmasūtrakāraiḥ svagrantheṣvāśritaḥ tena tatpratiṣedhe eva yatnosata kṛtaḥ nāṇvādikāraṇavādapratiṣedhe
te'pi tu brahmakāraṇavādapakṣasya pratipakṣatvātpratiṣeddhavyāḥ
smṛtyadhikaraṇam pṛṣṭham samanvayavirodhaparihāralakṣaṇayoḥ saṃgatipradarśanāya tātparyārthasaṃkṣepaḥ mokṣasādhanavyutpādanaparāṇām anuṣṭheye'vakāśamalabhamānānāṃ paramarṣibhiḥ kapilādibhiḥ praṇītānāṃ śiṣṭaiśca parigṛhītānāṃ smṛtīnāmanavakāśatvabhiyā tadavirodhenaiva vedāntā vyākhyātavyāḥ iti pūrvapakṣasya upanyāsa 'virodhe tvanapekṣaṃ syādasati hyanumānam' iti pūrvatantra siddhārthamavalambya anutthānaparāhata pūrvapakṣa iti śaṅkā kapilaprabhṛtīnāmārṣajñāne'pratiite śraddhājāḍyāt punarākṣepotthānasya samarthanam smṛtibalena pratyavatiṣṭhamānasya smṛtibalenaivottaraṃ pravakṣyāmītyataḥ īśvarakāraṇavādismṛtyantarānavakāśadoṣopanyāsa smṛtivigāne śrutyanusārismṛtiparigrahasyopapādanam kapilādismṛtīnāṃ pratyakṣamūlatvena prāmāṇyaśaṅkāyā nirasanam śraddhājaḍānāṃ śikṣaṇam saṃbhavatyanyasmin vaidike kapile śrutisāmānyamātreṇāvaidika kapilaḥ śrauta iti bhrama evāyamiti nirūpya 'ṛṣiṃ prasūtaṃ kapilam' ityādipratipattiśeṣasyāsādhakatvapratipādanam brahmavādināṃ manvādīnāṃ śrautatva pradarśanam pradhāne puruṣabhede cābhiniviśamānasya kāpiladarśanasya śrutismṛtivirodhaprapañcanena nigamanam alokavedaprasiddhatvāt mahadādīnāṃ ṣaṣṭhendriyārthakalpatā yogapratyuktyadhikaraṇam pūrvātideśena yogapratyākhyānam adhikāśaṅkayā pṛthagadhikaraṇārambhasya samarthanam sāṃkhyayogayorādarātiśaya eva tannirākaraṇe ādarātiśayasya heturiti pratipādanam aviṣaye'prāmāṇyaṃ sāṃkhyayogayoḥ puruṣaviśuddhinivṛttiniṣṭhādisvaviṣaye'pi prāmāṇyaṃ nopahanyāditi sāṃkhyayogayorarthaikadeśābhyanujñānam navilakṣaṇatvādhikaraṇam avāntarasaṃgatyarthamadhikaraṇasya virodhinyāyābhāsīkaraṇārthatvapradarśanam śrutitarkayorasamānaviṣayatvenāvirodhaśaṅkā samānaviṣayatvasamarthanena samādhi viṣayato'nubhavāntaraṅgatvasya mananavidhivihitatvasya ca tarkasamādaraṇahetutayopanyāsaḥ jaganna brahmaprakṛtikam tadvilakṣaṇatvāt ityanumānena pūrvapakṣaḥ vyāptisamarthanam JUR jagato'śuddhayacetanatvadarśanāt brahmavailakṣaṇyasya heto sādhanam cetanopakaraṇasya jagato'cetanatvasamarthanam acetanatvaṃ vyabhicaret cetanopakaraṇatā iti śaṅkāyāḥ samādhi śrutārthāpatyā samastasya jagataḥ cetanatvotprekṣaṇam 'tathātvaṃ ca śabdāt' iti prāṇā anūtkrāmanti 'iti vākyaṃ viṣayīkṛtya sūtradvayasya yojanāntaram prāṇāṇutvādhikaraṇam prāṇānāṃ sūkṣmatvaparicchinnatvayoḥ sādhanam prāṇa śreṣṭhayādhikaraṇam vāyukriyādhikaraṇam WAN prāṇaḥ prāṇasya jīvavatsvātantryasya vyāvartanam prāṇāntarāsaṃbhavidehendriyavidhāraṇakāraṇaṃ na tu paricchedadhāraṇādikaraṇam yenāsya viṣayāntaramanviṣyeta iti viṣayāntaraprasañjanasya nirākaraṇam svamahimnaiva prāṇāḥ pravarteran iti pūrvapakṣa agnyādyabhimāninībhirdevatābhiradhiṣṭhitaṃ vāgādikaraṇajātaṃ svakāryeṣu pravartate iti siddhāntaḥ adhiṣṭhātrīṇāṃ bhoktṛtvaprasaṅgasya śrutito nyāyataśca parihāraḥ svakarmārjite dehe jīvasya bhoktṛtāniyamāt śārīreṇaiva ca prāṇasaṃbandhasya nityatvāt devatā na bhoktṛpakṣasyeti nigamanam indriyādhikaraṇam śrutermukhyasyaivetare prāṇā vṛttibhedāḥ iti pūrvapakṣaḥ 'etasmājjāyate' ityādivyapadeśabhedāttattvāntarāṇīti siddhāntaḥ bhedaśrutilakṣaṇabheda yostattvāntaratvasādhakatayopanyāsaḥ  saṃjñāmūrtiklaptyadhikaraṇam 'anena jīvenātmanā' iti viśeṣaṇāt tāsāmanādaraṇīyatāpradarśanam vyātmakatvaṃ dvidhā vyākhyāya siddhāntahetoḥ sādhakatvasya samarthanam praśnaprativacanayorapśabdasya bhūyastvāpekṣatvasamarthanāya sarvadeheṣvapāṃ bāhulyasya dvidhā 'pañcamyāmāhutāvāṃ puruṣabhāvo na ghaṭate ityākṣepa pañcamyāmāhutāvapāṃ puruṣavacastvaprakāre pṛṣṭe prathamāyāmanapāṃ homāyopādātumaśakyāyāśca buddhiprasādalakṣaṇāyāḥ śraddhāyā hotavyatayābhidhānaṃ na kuta  ārambhaṇaśabdādibhyaḥ 
ārambhaṇaśabdastāvadekavijñānena sarvavijñānaṃ pratijñāya dṛṣṭāntāpekṣāyāmucyate 'yathā somyaikena mṛtpiṇḍena sarve mṛnmayaṃ vijñāta syādvācārambhaṇaṃ vikāro nāmadheyaṃ mṛttiketyeva satyam' iti 
etaduktaṃ bhavati ekena mṛtpiṇḍena paramārthato mṛdātmanā vijñātena sarve mṛnmayaṃ ghaṭaśarāvodañcanādikaṃ mṛdātmakatvāviśeṣādvijñātaṃ bhavet 
yato vācārambhaṇaṃ vikāro nāmadheyam vācaiva kevalamastītyārabhyate vikāra ghaṭa śarāva udaścanaṃ ceti

ārambhaṇaśabdādibhya ityāpā sū dvitīyo'dhyāyaḥ 
Seppear diśabdāt 'aitadātmyamidaṃ sarve tatsatyaṃ sa ātmā tattva masi' 'idaṃ sarve yadayamātmā brahmaivedaṃ sarvam ' 'ātmaived sarvam neha nānāsti kiṃcana 'ityevamādyapyātmaikatvapratipādanaparaṃ vacanajātamudāhartavyama

'yenāśruta śrutaṃ bhavatyamataṃ matamavijñātaṃ vijñātam' iti 'ātmani khalvare dṛṣṭe śrute mate vijñāte idaṃ sarve viditam' iti 'kasminnu bhagavo vijñāte sarvamidaṃ vijñātaṃ bhavati' iti  na kācana mahardhā vidyāsti' iti caivaṃrūpā prativedāntaṃ pratijñā vijñāyate

prāṇānāṃ ca dehāntarapratipattau gatiḥ śrāvyate'tamutkrāmantaṃ prāṇo'nutkrāmati prāṇamanūtkrāmantaṃ sarve prāṇā anūtkāmanti' ityādiśrutibhiḥ
sā ca prāṇānāṃ gatirnāśrayamantareṇa saṃbhavatītyataḥ prāṇagatiprayuktā tadāśrayabhūtānāmapāmapi bhūtāntaropasṛṣṭānāṃ gatirarthādvagamyate
na hi nirāśrayā prāṇā kacidgacchanti tiṣṭhanti vā jīvato darśanāt 
agnyādigatiśruteriti cenna bhāktatvāt 
syādetat  naiva prāṇā dehāntarapratipattau saha jīvena gacchanti agnyādigatiśruteḥ 
tathā hi śruti maraṇakāle vāgādaya prāṇā agnyādīndevāngacchantīti darśayati'yatrāsya puruṣasya mṛtasyāgniṃ vāgadhyeti vātaṃ prāṇaḥ' ityādinā iti cet na bhāktatvāt
vāgādīnāmagnyādigatiśrutirgauṇī lomasu keśeṣu ca adarśanāt'oṣadhīrlomāni vanaspatīnke sūtrabhāṣye pā śā 'iti hi tavāmnāyate na hi lomāni keśācotluya oṣadhīrvanaspatīṃca gacchantīti saṃbhavati
na ca jīvasya prāṇopādhipratyākhyāne gamanamavakalpate

prathame'śravaṇāditi cenna tā eva hyupapatteḥ 
syādetat kathaṃ puna 'pañcamyāmāhutāvāpaḥ puruṣavacaso bhavanti' ityetat nirdhārayituṃ pāryate yāvatā naiva prathame'gnāvapāṃ śravaṇamasti  iha hi lokaprabhṛtayaḥ pañcāgnayaḥ pañcānāmāhutīnāmādhāratvenādhītā 
teṣāṃ ca pramukhe 'asau vāva loko gautamāgni 'ityupanyasya 'tasminne tasminnannau devā śraddhāṃ juhvati' iti śraddhā homyadravyatvena āveditā
na tatra āpo homyadravyatayā śrutā 
yadi nāma parjanyādiṣūttareṣu caturdhvagnidhvapāṃ homyadravyatā parikalpyeta parikalpyatāṃ nāma teṣu hotavyatayopāttānāṃ somādīnāmabahulatvopapatte

sāhasametat

tasmādayuktaḥ pañcamyāmāhutāvapāṃ puruṣabhāva iti cet naiṣa doṣaḥ 
hi yataḥ tatrāpi prathame'gnau tā evāpaḥ śraddhāśabdenābhipreyante 
kuta  upapatte 
evaṃ hyādimadhyāvasānasaṃgānāt anākulametadekavākyamupapadyate

' iti tu pañcamyāmāhutāvāpa puruṣava caso bhavanti' iti ca upasaṃharan etadeva darśayati

sā ca śraddhāyā aptve yukti 
kāraṇānurūpaṃ hi kārya bhavati 
na ca śraddhākhya pratyayaḥ manaso jīvasya vā dharma san dharmiṇo niṣkṛṣya homāyopādātuṃ śakyate paśvādibhya iva hṛdayādīni iti āpa eva śraddhāśabdā bhaveyuḥ 
śraddhāśabdaścāpsūpapadyate vaidikaprayogadarśanāt 'śraddhā vā āpa 'iti

aśrutatvāditi cenneṣṭādikāriṇāṃ pratīteḥ 
pondo athāpi syāt  praśnaprativacanābhyāṃ nāma āpa śraddhādikrameṇa pañcamyāmāhutau puruṣākāraṃ pratipadyeran
na tu tatsaṃpariṣvaktā jīvā raheyuḥ aśrutatvāt na hyatra apāmiva jīvānāṃ śrāvayitā kaścicchabdo'sti

kuta  iṣṭādikāriṇāṃ pratīte atha ya ime grāma iṣṭāpūrte dattamityupāsate te dhūmamabhisaṃbhavanti' ityupakramya iṣṭādikāriṇāṃ dhūmādinā pitṛyāṇena pathā candraprāptiṃ kathayati 'ākāśācandramasameṣa somo rājā' iti 
ta evehāpi pratīyante 'tasminnetasminnannau devā śraddhāṃ juhvati takhā āhuteḥ somo rājā saṃbhavati' iti śrutisāmānyāt 
teṣāṃ ca agnihotradarśapūrṇamāsādikarmasādhanabhūtā dadhipayaḥprabhṛtayo dravadravyabhūyastvātpratyakṣameva āpaḥ santi

' asau svargāya lokāya svāhā' iti
tatastā śraddhāpūrvaka karmasamavāyinya āhutimayya āpo'pūrvarūpā satyaḥ tāniṭādikāriṇo jīvānpariveṣṭya amuṃ lokaṃ phaladānāya nayantī ti yat tadatra juhotinā abhidhīyate śraddhāṃ juhvatīti 
tathā ca agnihotre ṣaṭpranīnirvacanarūpeṇa vākyaśeṣeṇa 'te vā ete āhutī hute utkrāmata 'ityevamādinā agnihotrāhutyoḥ phalārambhāya lokāntaraprāptidarśitā 
tasmādāhutīmayībhiradbhiḥ saṃpariṣvaktā jīvā rahanti svakarmaphalopabhogāyeti te 
kathaṃ punaridamiṣṭādikāriṇāṃ svakarmaphalopabhogāya raṃhaṇaṃ pratijñāyate yāvatā teṣāṃ dhūmapratīkena vartsanā candramasamadhirūḍhānāmannabhāvaṃ darśayati'eṣa somo rājā taddevānāmantraṃ taṃ tevā bhakṣayanti' iti 'te candraṃ prāpyānnaṃ bhavanti tāṃstatra devā yathā somaṃ rājānamāpyāyasvāpakṣīya svetyevametāṃstatra bhadhyanti' iti ca samānaviṣayaṃ śrutyantaram  na ca vyāghrādibhiriva devairbhakṣyamāṇānāmupabhoga saṃbhavatīti

bhāktameṣāmannatvam na mukhyam

candramaṇḍale cediṣṭādikāriṇāmupabhokimarthamadhikāriṇa iṣṭādi āyāsabahulaṃ karma kuryuḥ

kṛtātyaye'nuśayavāndṛṣṭasmṛtibhyāṃ yathetamanevaṃ ca

yena karmabṛndena candramasamārūḍhāḥ phalopabhogāya tasminnupabhogena kṣayite teṣāṃ yadammayaṃ śarīraṃ candramasyupabhogāyārabdham tat upabhogakṣayadarśanaśokāgnisaṃparkātpravilīyate savitṛkiraṇasaṃparkādiva himakarakāḥ hutabhugarci saṃparkādiva ca ghṛtakāṭhinyam

kena hetunā  dṛṣṭasmṛtibhyāmityāha 
tathā hi pratyakṣā śruti sānuśayānāmavarohaṃ darśayati' tadya iha ramaṇīyacaraṇā abhyāśo ha yatte ramaṇīyāṃ yonimāpadyeranbrāhmaṇayoniṃ vā kṣatriyayoniṃ vā vaiśyayoniṃ vātha ya iha kapūyacaraṇā abhyāśo ha yatte kapūyāṃ yonimāpadyerañśvayoniṃ vā sūkarayoniṃ vā cāṇḍālayoniṃ vā' iti 
caraṇaśabdenānuśaya sūcyata iti varṇayiṣyati 
dṛṣṭaścāyaṃ janmanaiva pratiprāṇyuccāvacarūpa upabhoga pravibhajyamāna ākasmikatvāsaṃbhavādanuśayasadbhāvaṃ sūcayati abhyudayapratyavāyayo sukṛtaduṣkṛtahetutvasya sāmānyataḥ śāstreṇāvagamitatvāt

kaḥ punaranuśayo nāmetikecittāvadāhuḥ svargārthasya karmaṇo bhuktaphalakhāvaśeṣaḥ kaścidanuśayo nāma bhāṇḍānusārisnehavat yathā hi snehabhāṇḍaṃ ricyamānaṃ na sarvātmanā ricyate bhāṇḍānusāryeva kaścitsnehaśeṣo'vatiṣṭhate tathā anuśayo'pīti

nāyaṃ doṣa 
na hi sarvātmanā bhuktaphalatvaṃ karmaṇa pratijānīmahe

te tu saṃyamanaṃ yamālayamavagāhya svaduṣkṛtānurūpā yāmīryātanā anubhūya punareva imaṃ lokaṃ pratyavarohanti

kuta  tadgatidarśanāt
tathā hi yamavacanasarūpā śruti prayatām aniṣṭādikāriṇāṃ yamavaśyatāṃ darśayati 'na sāṃparāya pratibhāti bālaṃ pramādyantaṃ vittamohena mūḍham 
ayaṃ loko nāsti para iti mānī puna punarvaśamāpadyate me' iti

smaranti ca

api ca sapta 
api ca sapta narakā rauravapramukhā duṣkṛtaphalopabhogabhūmitvena smaryante paurāṇikai 
tānaniṣṭādikāriṇa prāpnuvanti

pā nanu viruddhamidamayamāyattā yātanāḥ pāpakarmāṇo'nubhavantīti yāvatā teṣu rauravādiṣu anye citraguptādayo nānādhiṣṭhātāra smaryanta iti 
netyāha tatrāpi ca tadvyāpārāvirodhaḥ

vidyākarmaṇoriti tu prakṛtatvāt 
pañcāgnividyāyām 'vettha yathāsau loko na saṃpūryate' ityasya praśnasya prativacanāvasare śrūyate 'athaitayoḥ pathorna katareṇacana tānīmāni kṣudrāṇyasakṛdāvartīni bhūtāni bhavanti 
jāyasva mriyastvetyetattṛtīyaṃ sthānaṃ tenāsau lokosū tṛtīyo'dhyāyaḥ 
na saṃpūryate' iti 
tatra etayoḥ pathoriti vidyākarmaṇorityetat 
kasmāt  prakṛtatvāt 
vidyākarmaṇī hi devayānapitṛyāṇayoḥ patho pratipade prakṛte'tadya itthaṃ viduḥ' iti vidyā tayā pratipattavyo devayānaḥ panthāḥ prakīrtitaḥ 
'iṣṭāpūrte dattam' iti karma tena pratipattavyaḥ pitṛyāṇa panthāḥ prakīrtita tatprakriyāyām 'athaitayoḥ pathorna katareṇacana' iti śrutam 
etaduktaṃ bhavati ye na vidyāsādhanena devayāne pathyadhikṛtāḥ nāpi karmaṇā pitṛyāṇe teṣāmeṣa kṣudrajantulakṣaṇo'sakṛdāvartī tṛtīyaḥ panthā bhavatīti

tena anārohādeva asaṃpūraṇamiti yuktam 
MET pā avarohasyeṣṭādikāriṣvapyaviśiṣṭatve sati tṛtīyasthānoktyānarthakyaprasaṅgāt

na tṛtīye sthāne dehalābhāya pañcasaṃkhyāniyama āhutīnāmādartavyaḥ
kutaḥ tathopalabdhe

api ca pañcamyāmāhutāvāpaḥ puruṣavacaso bhavanti' iti manuṣyaśarīrahetutvena āhutisaṃkhyā kīrtyate na kīṭapataṅgādiśarīrahetutvena puruṣaśabdasya manuṣyajātivacanatvāt

pavādayocaṃ vyavasthitaviṣayatvam 
tasmādviśuddhaṃ karma vaidina śiṣṭairanuṣṭhīyamānatvāt anindyamānatvācca
tena na tasya kam pratirūpaṃ phalam jātisthāvaratvam 
na ca śvādijanmavadapi vrīhyādijanma bhavitumarhati
taddhi kapūyacaraṇānadhikṛtya ucyate
naivamiha vaiśeṣikaḥ kaścidhikāro'sti 
ataścandrasthalaskhalitānāmanuśāyināṃ brīhyādisaṃśleṣamātraṃ tadbhāva ityu pacaryate 
retaḥ sigyogo'tha 
itaśca vrīhyādisaṃśleṣamātraṃ tadbhāvaḥ yatkāraṇaṃ vrīhyādibhāvasyānantaramanuśayināṃ retaḥ sigbhāva āmnāyate'yo yo hyanamatti yo reta siñcati tadbhūya eva bhavati' iti 
na cātra mukhyo reta sigbhāva saṃbhavati
cirajāto hi prāptayauvano reta sigbhavati
kathamiva anupacaritaṃ tadbhāvam adyamānānānugato'nuśayī pratipadyate  tatra tāvadavaśyaṃ reta sigyoga eva reta sigbhāvo'bhyupagantavyaḥ
tadvat trīhyādibhāvo'pi vrīhyādiyoga evetyavirodhaḥ 
yone śarīram 
atha reta sigbhāvasthānantaraṃ yonau niṣikte retasi yoneradhi śarīram anuśayinām anuśayaphalopabhogāya jāyatasūtrabhāṣye prā ityāha śāstram tadya iha ramaṇīyacaraṇā' ityādi
tasmā dapya vagamyatenāvarohe brīhyādibhāvāvasare taccharīrameva sukhaduḥkhānvitaṃ bhavatīti 
tasmāt śrīhyādisaṃśleṣamātramanuśayināṃ tajjanmeti siddham 
iti śrīmatparamahaṃsaparivrājakācāryasya śrīgovindabhagavatpūjyapādaśiṣyasya śrīmacchaṃkarabhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīrakamīmāṃsāsūtrabhāṣye tṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ

śrīḥ 

viṣayānukramaṇikā 
tṛtīyo'dhyāyaḥ dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ tattvaṃ padārthavivekaḥ  saṃdhyādhikaraṇam saṃgatipradarśanapūrvakam uddeśyaṃ tvaṃ padārtha vivecayitum 'atha rathān 'iti śrutimavaṣṭabhya tathyarūpāṃ svapnasṛṣṭimudāhṛtya mithyāpratyayā sarve'pi samyañca iti pratijānānāṃ pūrvavādināṃ pakṣasya udbhāvanam 'ya eṣa supteṣu 'ityādikāṭhakaśrutimavalambya prājñakartṛkatvaṃ hetukṛtya svapnasṛṣṭe pāramārthikatvasādhanam vyāpaka viruddhopanyāsena vastutvaṃ vyāvartya māyāmātratvasiddhāntaḥ pṛṣṭham śubhāśubhaphalānvayavyatirekābhyāṃ śāstreṇa ca vi rodhasya parihāra svayaṃ jyotiṣṭavivecanānuguṇaṃ rathādyabhāvavacanameva śrutyā vyākhyeyam sthādisṛṣṭivacanaṃ tu bhaktyā iti vivicya paroktanirasanam prājñakartṛkatvasya parābhimatahetoḥ asiddhibādhābhyāmābhāsīkaraṇam paramātmāṃśasya jīvasya satyasaṃkalpasya sāṃkalpikī svapne sthādisṛṣṭiiti śaṅkāyāḥ jīvasya jñānaiśvaryatirodhānamupapādya parihāra tadbhāvādhikaraṇama suṣuptiparīkṣārthī viṣayopanyāsaḥ nāḍīpurītatparamātmanāṃ suṣutasthānatayā śrayamāṇānām ekārthānāṃ vikalpe brahmabhāvāniyamāt karmaṇaivāpavarga saṃbhāvayatāṃ pūrvavādināṃ matasya udbhāvanam samuccayena nāḍyādīni svāpāya upasarpatīti siddhāntaḥ ekavi bhaktinirdeśasya anaikāntikatvapradarśanam sāpekṣaśrutyanurodhena nirapekṣaśrutiṃ nītvā samuccayabādhanirasanam jīvasyādheyatvamabhyupagataṃ parityajya brahmātmatvameva jīvasya suṣute brahmādhāratvam tadupādhika raṇamātrādhāratayā tu jīvasya suṣusārambhāya nāḍīpurītadādhāratvam iti atulyārthatānirū paṇena vikalpavighaṭanam asatyapavāde jīvasyautsargikaṃ brahmatādātmyaṃ na suṣupte anyathayituṃ śakyamiti vikalpāyoge yuktyantaram paramātmātirikteṣu sthāneṣu viśeṣavijñānasyāvaśya katayā suteranupapattiḥ guṇapradhānabhāvena samuccayaḥ na samapradhānatayeti niṣkarṣa ātmanaḥ prabodhāpādānatāṃ svāpādhikāre śiṣyamāṇāmupanyamya siddhāntaṃdṛḍhīkaraṇam karmānusmṛtiśabda vidhyadhikaraṇam jalabindunyāyena supta evaṃ pratibudhyata iti na niyantuṃ śakyateiti pūrvapakṣa karmaśeṣānuṣṭhānadarśanam anusmṛtiṃ śrutiṃ karmavidyā vidhyanupapatti copanyasya suptasyaiva punarutthānamiti niyamasya samarthanam utsūtraṃ siddhāntayuktiviśeṣāṇāmupanyāsaḥ vivekahetoḥ karmaṇo'vidyāyāśca sadbhāvāt jīvasya brahmābhedāca jalabindunyāyasya vighaṭanam  mugdhādhikaraṇama prasiddhāvasthānāṃ mūrchā anyatameti pūrvapakṣaḥ dehadhāraṇābhāvāt viṣayamātrānupalabdheśca mugdhasya jāgrato vailakṣaṇyasamarthanam niḥsaṃjñakatvāt prāṇoṣmaṇorbhāvācca svapnamṛtibhyāṃ mūrchāyā bhedasya pratipādanam suṣuptamohayo prayojanakāraṇalakṣaṇabhedebhyo bhedasya samarthanam ardhena suṣuptapakṣasya bhavati mugdhatvam ardhena avasthāntarapakṣasya iti siddhāntaḥ ubhayaliṅgādhikaraṇam tatpadārthanirūpaṇārambhe pratijñā bhinnākārayogo brahmaṇaḥ śāstrīya iti śaṅkāyābhedasya upāsanārthatvāt abhede tātparyāt neti nirasanam tatpradhānatvaṃ vinigamakamāśritya anākārabrahmāvadhāraṇam prakāśadṛṣṭāntena aupādhikamākārayogamanākāreubhayaliṅga śrutyupanyāsena saṃśayabījodghāṭanam svata upādhito vā parasya brahmaṇaḥ ubhayaliṅgatvānupapatternirviśeṣameva pratipattavyam iti siddhānta 'pyupāsanārtha samarthya ākāravadviṣayāṇāmapi śrutīnāṃ gatipradarśanam nirviśeṣatvānukūlatayā anyāpoha mugvena brahma darśayantīnāṃ śrutismṛtīnām upanyāsaḥ jalasūryakādiśāstrīyadṛṣṭāntasya prakṛtānukūlatayā ekaniyogapratīteḥ brahmopāsanāvākyānā mekavākyatetyabhimānasya acodanātantratvādbrahmavijñānaṃ prapañca pravilayaṃ ca aśakyatvāt anupapatteḥ anyathāsiddhatvācca niyogagocarādapanīya śithi līkaraṇam upanyāsaḥ uktadṛṣṭāntavaiṣamyaśaṅkā tatpratividhānaṃ ca anupraveśaśrutyupanyāsena uktadṛṣṭāntadṛḍhīkaraṇam niṣprapañcatvaparatayā sanmātratvaparatayā ca adhikaraṇadvayaṃ kalpayatāṃ svayūthyānāṃ matasyodbhāvanam evamadhikaraṇāntarārambhasya sarvathā vaiyarthyamiti tannirasanam ākāra śrutīnāmapi taditarākārapravilayo gatiriti matamanūdya brahmopāsanāvākyānāṃ pārthagarthyasamarthanena tannirasanam prapañcapakṣe ucchedāt brahmapakṣa aniyojyatvāt jīvasya niyojyatāvighaṭanena niyogavārtāyā vārtīkaraṇam niyogābhyupagame'pi sādhyānubandhabhedādekaniyogatvamasiddhamiti nigamanam prakṛtaitāvattvādhikaraṇam neti netīti pratiṣedhe saṃśayamupanyasya brahmāpi brahmaiva vā pratiṣedhyam iti pakṣayoḥ sahetukamupanyāsaḥ na hyanāśrayaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ śakyaḥ pratipattum 
na ca brahmapare śabde brahmaṇi pramāṇe sati tatpratiṣedho'pi pramāṇavān 
nāpi vedāntā brahma pratiṣedhāyaiva mahatā prayatnena pratipādayanti iti tayoḥ pakṣayornirasanam 'prakṛtaitāvatvaṃ hi pratiṣedhatīti sūtrāvayavavibhajanam mūrtāmūrtaviṣayatayā bhūtarāśivāsanārāśiviṣayatayā kṛtsnaviṣayapratiṣedhaparyavasāyivīṃ sārūpatayā ca pratiṣedhadvayasya nayanam 'na hyetasmāditi netyanyatparamasti 'iti vākyaṃ etasmādityasya ādiṣṭādeśanaparāmarśitayā vākyabhedena vākyaikyena ca dvidhā yojayitvā tadanurodhena 'tato bravīti ca bhūyaḥ 'ityasya anyatparamastītyetadviṣayatayā atha nāmadheyamityetadviṣayatayā ca vibhajanam abhāvo na brahmābhāve kramate ayogyatvādityatra śrutismṛtibhyāṃ hetoḥ sādhanam śrutismṛtibhyāṃ brahmaṇaḥ saṃrādhanagrāhyatāpradarśanam saṃrādhyasaṃrādhakabhāve jīvaprājñayorahikuṇḍalavat pra kāśāśrayavacca bhedābhedayorbhāvikayorevāvirodhaṃ matāntaraṃ nirasya cidātmana aupādhikabhedabhāne'pi svata ekarasatvameveti advaitaniṣkarṣeṇa nigamanam parādhikaraṇama phalādhikaraṇam setūnmānasaṃbandhabhedavyapadeśānāṃ vyākhyānapuraḥsaraṃ brahmaṇo'nyattatvamastīti pūrvapakṣasyodbhāvanam setuvyapadeśasya vidhārakatvasāmānyaparatayā parihāraḥ unmānavyapadeśasya ādhyānārthatayā parihāra saṃbandhabhedavyapadeśayoraupādhikatayā parihāra anyapratiṣedhasamāśrayaṇa eva sarvaṃgatatvamanyātmanaḥ prāmāṇikamupapadyate iti upasaṃhāraḥ upapatteḥ śruteśca īśvara eva phalaheturiti siddhāntenopakramaḥ karmaṇo vā sūkṣmā kāciduttarāvasthā phalasya vā pūrvāvasthā apūrva nāma kalpyamānaṃ vidhiviṣayasya yāgasya phalotpādakatvamupapādayatīti jaimini matasyodbhāvanam apūrvāgrahaṃ vihāya īśvaraprasādo'nurudhyatām 
karmāpekṣādapūrvāpekṣādvā īśvarāt phalamiti suviśadaṃ bhavet iti bādarāyaṇaniṣkarṣaḥ tṛtīya pādaguṇopasaṃhāraḥ sarvavedāntapratyayādhikaraṇama nirupādhibrahmatattvagocaraṃ vijñānaṃ manvānasya bhedābhedacintāvatārākṣepaḥ sopādhikabrahmaprāṇādiviṣayāsu upāsanāsu bhedābhedavimarśa upapanna iti parihāra nāmarūpadharmaviśeṣapunaruktiprabhṛtīnāṃ bhedahetūnāmupalambhāt prativedāntaṃ vijñānabheda iti pūrvapakṣaḥ saṃyogarūpacodanākhyāviśeṣāt vijñānānāṃ sarvavedāntapratyayatvamiti siddhāntaḥ pañcābhividyāprāṇasaṃvādādiṣu utpattigata eva guṇabhedo vaiśvadevīvat kathaṃ na bhindyāt iti viśeṣāśaṅkāyāḥ parihāraḥ śirovratasya svādhyāyadharmatvopapādanena vidyābhedakatvavighaṭanam prāyadarśananyāyena upāsanānāmapi sarvavedāntapratyayatvasiddhiḥ ityupasaṃhāraḥ upasaṃhārādhikaraṇam sarvavedāntapratyayatve sarvavijñānānāṃ guṇopasaṃhāraḥ phalamiti nirṇaya vyāptyadhikaraṇama anyathātvādhikaraṇama vedyabhedanirūpaṇena vājināṃ chandogānāṃ ca udgīthavidyā arthavādasaṃjñāsāmye'pi bhinnā iti niṣkarṣaḥ sarvābhedādhikaraṇama omityetadakṣaramityatra sāmānādhikaraṇye adhyāsāpavādakatvaviśeṣaṇapakṣāṇāṃ nirūpaṇam gauṇyā lakṣaṇāto durbalatvāt niṣphalatvāt padāntaravaiyarthyācca adhyāsāpavādakatvapakṣān nirasya viśeṣaṇapakṣeṇa siddhāntaḥ ānandādyadhikaraṇama prāṇasaṃvāde vasiṣṭhatvādiguṇānāmanuktānāmapi ekapradhānasaṃbaddhānāṃ koṣītakibrāhmaṇagatena evaṃśabdena parāmraṣṭuṃ yogyatvādupasaṃhāra iti nirṇa vāstavānāṃ vidheyānāṃ ca guṇānāṃ vastudharmatayā ca anuṣṭheyatayā ca avyavasthāvyavasthe vyavatiṣṭhete iti vivecanam ādhyānādhikaraṇam indriyebhyaḥ parā hyarthāḥ' ityādikāṭhakaśrutau sarveṣāmeva arthādīnāṃ paratvaṃ pratipipādayiṣitamiti pūrvapakṣaḥ dṛṣṭaprayojanatvāt ādarātiśayācca puruṣaparatvaprati pādanārtho'yaṃ saṃdarbha iti siddhāntaḥ ātmagṛhītyadhikaraṇam ātmāvā idameka eva' ityāditaittirīyakaśrutau lokasṛṣṭivacanāt sūtrātmaivābhilapyate iti pūrvapakṣa ākāśapūrvikāyāṃ sṛṣṭau yathā kvacittejapūrvikāyāḥ sṛṣṭerabhidhānaṃ tathā mahābhūtasṛṣṭayanabhidhānena lokasṛṣṭayabhidhānaṃ na virudhyate paramātmagrahaṇa eva prāgutpatterātmaikatvāvadhāraṇamāñjasamavaṃkalpate iti paramātmaivābhilapyate iti siddhāntaḥ sadupakramasya chāndogyagatasya saṃdarbhasya ātmopakramasya ca vājasaneyakagatasya kimaikārthyam āhosvidarthabheda iti saṃśayopanyāsena kalpāntarārambhaḥ āmnānatantratvādarthaparigrahasya upakramatantratvādupasaṃhārasya arthabheda evocitaḥ tādātmyopadeśaśca saṃpattiparatayā neya iti pūrvapakṣaḥ sadeva ' 'ekameva 'ityādyavadhāraṇaṃ tādātmyapratipādanāyāmevāvakalpate na tādātmyasaṃpādanāyām 
sāmānyopakramaśca na vākyaśeṣagatena viśegheṇa virudhyate
sacchabdārtho'pi na mukhyādātmano'nyaḥ saṃbhavati iti pratipādyābheda iti siddhāntaḥ kāryākhyānādhikaraṇam chandogānāṃ vājasaneyināṃ ca prāṇavidyāprakaraṇe yat aśiśiṣatām aśitavatāṃ ca ubhayata ācamanam anagnatācintanaṃ ca pratīyate tadubhayamapi vidhīyate apūrvatvāt vispaṣṭavidhivibhaktikatvādvā ācamanameva vidhīyate iti pakṣayorudbhāvanam A smārtasya ācamanasya vyāpakatvāt dṛṣṭisāhacaryā t samidho yajatītyādivat vartamānāpadeśasyāpi vidhikṣamatvāt 'jartilayavāgvā vā juhuam yāt' ityādivat vidhivibhakterapi avivakṣitatvasaṃbhavācca vāsovijñānameva vidhīyate nācamanam iti siddhāntaḥ samānādhikaraṇama agnirahasyabṛhadāraṇyakayo śāṇḍilyavidyā a bhyāsādhikaraṇanyāyena bhinnati pūrvapakṣaḥ samānaguṇapunaḥśravaṇasya viprakṛṣṭavidyāpratyabhijñāpakatvenānyaparatvasaṃbhavādabhyāsādhikaraṇanyāyāpravṛtte vidyaikatvamiti siddhāntaḥ saṃbandhādhikaraṇam saṃbhṛtyadhikaraṇam bṛhadāraṇyake satyavidyāyāmādiśyamānayorupani do saṃkara iti svarūpamātraprādhānyābhiprāyeṇa pūrvapakṣaḥ saviśeṣaṇasyaiva pradhānatvāt atideśaliṅgācca tayovrvyavastheti siddhāntaḥ iti siddhāntaḥ saṃbhṛtyādīnāṃ guṇānāṃ śāṇḍilyādividyāsu ṣoḍaśakalādividyāsu ca pratyabhijñāsaṃbhavādupasaṃhāra iti pūrvapakṣaḥ asādhāraṇadharmāṇāmapratyabhijñānādanupasaṃhāra puruṣavidyādhikaraṇam vedhādyadhikaraṇama taittirīyakatāṇḍinoḥ puruṣavidyā puruṣayajñatvamaragāvabhṛthatvādisāmyādekaivaiti pūrvapakṣa bhūyovalakṣaṇyānna vidyekyamiti siddhāntaḥ hānyadhikaraṇam vidyāsaṃnidhipaṭhitānāṃ pravidhyādimantrāṇāṃ pravargyādikarmaṇāṃ ca anyatra viniyuktānāmapi saṃnighisāmarthyāt vidyārthatvenāpi pratipattiḥ bṛhaspatisavadṛṣṭāntena khādiratvādidṛṣṭāntena vā iti pūrvapakṣa prabalaiḥ śrutyādibhiranyatra viniyuktānām avirodhe'pi durbalasaṃnidhimātreṇa na saṃbhavati vi grāsu viniyogaḥ iti siddhāntaḥ yatra hānamātraṃ sukṛtaduṣkṛtayoḥ śrūyate tatra aśrūyamāṇaṃ vidyāntaragocaraśākhāntaṃrīyaśravaṇaviṣayamapyupāyanamanavaśyaṃ bhāvi na saṃnipatet iti pūrvapakṣaḥ ekaviṃśādivādavat arthavādāntarāpekṣārthavādāntarapravṛtte saṃbhavāt aṣṭadoṣaduṣṭavikalpaprasaṅgabhayena kuśādivat vākyāntarasya vākyāntaraśeṣatvasya aucityācca hānaśabdaśeṣa upāyanaśabda upāyanamanuvartayati kevalahānaśravaṇe'pi stutiprakarṣāya iti siddhāntaḥ vidhūnanaśrutau vidhūnanaṃ cālanameveti prāpte vākyaśeṣe upāyanaśravaṇabalāt hānameveti nirṇaya iti varṇakāntaram sāṃparāyādhikaraṇam yathāśruti ardhapatha eva sukṛtaduṣkṛtavimokaḥ prati pattavyaḥ evaṃ ca na paryavidyatastatprakṣaya iti pūrvapakṣa pāṭhakramādbalīyāṃsau śrūtyarthāvanurudhya samarthasya kṣepāyogāt maraṇāt prāgeva sukṛtaduṣkṛtakṣaya iti siddhānta gaterarthavattvādhikaraṇam aniyamādhikaraṇama upāstivat bodho'pi gatimān iti pūrvapakṣaḥ prāptiphalakasyopāsanasya gatimattve'pi svāsthyaphale bodhe vyarthā gatirna saṃnipatet iti siddhāntaḥ yāsu vidyāsu panthāḥ śrūyate tāsveva prakaraṇabalāt sa niyamyeta  iti pūrvapakṣaḥ 'ye ceme' 'śuklakṛṣṇe' ityādi śrutismṛtibhyāṃ prakaraṇasya bādhāt sarvāsāmeva saguṇavidyānāṃ panthāḥ iti siddhāntaḥ yāvadadhikārādhikaraṇam apāntaratabhaḥprabhṛtīnāṃ dehāntarotpattidarśanāt brahmavidyāyā pākṣikaṃ mokṣahetutvam ahetutvaṃ iti pūrvapakṣa vāyāvadadhikāramādhikārikā avatiṣṭhate tadavasāne ca apavṛjyanteityupapannatvāt viduṣa kevalyasiddhiraikāntikī iti siddhāntaḥ akṣaradhyadhikaraṇam iyadhikaraṇam pradhānatantrāṇāmaṅgānāmiva akṣaratantrāṇāṃ pratiṣedharūpāṇāṃ viśeṣaṇānāmapi yatra kvacidamyutpannānāṃ sarvatrākṣareṇābhisaṃbandhaḥ iti ānandādayaḥ pradhānasyatyasya prapañcaḥ chatrinyāyavākyaśeṣanyāyayo mukhyārthasaṃbhavenānavatārāt dvā suparṇetyatra ṛtaṃ pibantāvityatra ca vedyabhedena vidyābheda iti pūrvapakṣaḥ upakramopasaṃhārānurodhena madhyasyāpi neyatvāt aikavidyam iti siddhāntaḥ asya yogasya BE puruṣa sabāhyābhyantaro hyaja tadetadbrahmāpūrvamanaparamanantaramabāhyamayamātmā brahma sarvānubhūḥ' ityevamādīni vākyāni niṣprapañcabrahmātmatattvapradhānāni na arthāntarapradhānāni ityetatpratiṣṭhāpitam 'tattu samanvayāt' ityatra

yadi tāvadanekaliṅgatvaṃ parasya brahmaṇo nirākartavyamityayaṃ prayāsaḥ tata pūrveṇaiva 'na sthānato'pi' ityanenādhikaraṇena nirākṛtamiti uttaramadhikaraṇam 'prakāśavacca' ityetadvyarthameva bhavet 
na ca sallakṣaṇameva brahma na bodhalakṣaṇama iti śakyaṃ vaktuma 'vijñānaghana eva' ityādiśrutivaiyarthyaprasaṅgāta
kathaṃ vā nirastacaitanyaṃ brahma cetanasya jīvasyātmatvenopadiśyeta  nāpi bodhalakṣaṇameva brahma na sallakṣaṇam iti śakyaṃ vaktum astītyevopalabdhatryaḥ' ityādiśrutivaiyarthyaprasa ṅgāt 
kathaṃ vā nirastasattāko bodho'bhyupagamyeta 
nāpyubhayalakṣaṇameva brahmaiti śakyaṃ vaktum pūrvābhyupagamavirodhaprasaṅgāt
sattāvyāvṛttena ca bodhena bodhavyāvṛttayā ca sattayā upetaṃ brahma pratijñānānasya tadeva pūrvādhikaraṇapratiṣiddhaṃ saprapañcatvaṃ prasajyeta 
śrutatvādadoṣa iti cet na ekasya anekasvabhāvatvānupapatteḥ 
atha sattaiva bodha bodha eva ca sattā nānayoḥ parasparavyāvṛttirastīti yayucyeta tathāpi kiṃ sallakṣaṇaṃ brahma uta bodhalakṣaṇam utobhayalakṣaṇam ityayaṃ vikalpo nirālambana eva syāt

kādhikaraṇatvenaivāsmābhirnītāni

katham  ye hi paravidyādhikāre kecitprapañcā ucyante yathā' yuktā hyasya haraya śatā daśeti ayaṃ vai harayo'yaṃ vai daśa ca sahasrāṇi bahūni cānantāni ca 'ityevamādaya te bhavantu pravilayārthā

yadetat nirastasamastaprapañcaṃ brahma nirdhāritam asmātparam anyattattvamasti nāstīti śrutivipratipatteḥ saṃśaya 
kāniciddhi vākyāni āpātenaiva pratibhāsamānāni brahmaṇo'pi param anyattattvaṃ pratipādayantīva
teṣāṃ hi parihāramabhidhātumayamupakramaḥ kriyate paramataḥ setūnmānasaṃbandhabhedvyapadeśebhyaḥ 
param ato brahmaṇaḥ anyattattvaṃ bhavitumarhati
kuta  setuvyapadeśāt unmānavyapadeśāt saṃbandhavyapadeśāt bhedavyapadeśācca 
setuvyapadeśastāvat' atha ya ātmā sa seturvivṛti 'ityātmaśabdābhihitasya brahmaṇaḥ setutvaṃ saṃkīrtayati 
setuśabdaśca hi loke jalasaṃtānavicchedakare mṛddārvā dipracaye prasiddha 
iha ca setuśabda ātmani prayukta iti laukikasetoriva ātmasetoranyasya vastuno'stitvaṃ gamayati sūtrabhāṣye pā setuṃ tīva' iti ca taratiśabdaprayogātyathā laukikaṃ setuṃ tīrtvā jāṅgalamasetuṃ prāpnoti evamātmānaṃ setuṃ tīva anātmānamasetuṃ prāpnotīti gamyate 
unmānavyapadeśaśca bhavati  tadetadbrahma catuṣpāt aṣṭāśaphaṃ ṣoḍaśakalamiti
yacca loke unmitam etāvadidamiti paricchinnaṃ kārṣāpaṇādi tato'nyadvastvastīti prasiddham 
tathā brahmaṇo'pyunmānāt tato'nyena vastunā bhavitavyamiti gamyate 
tathā saṃbandhavyapadeśo bhavati 'satā somya tadā saṃpanno bhavati' iti śārīra ātmā 'prājñenātmanā saṃpariṣvakta 'iti ca 
mitānāṃ ca mitena saṃbandho dṛṣṭaḥ yathā narāṇāṃ nagareṇa
jīvānāṃ ca brahmaṇā saṃbandhaṃ vyapadiśati suṣuptau
ata tata paramanyadamitamastīti gamyate 
bhedavyapadeśaśca enama gamayati
tathā hi  'atha ya eṣo'ntarāditye hiraṇmaya puruṣo dṛśyate' ityādityādhāramīśvaraṃ vyapadiśya tato bhedena akṣyādhāramīśvaraṃ vyapadiśati' atha ya eṣo'kṣiṇi puruṣo dṛśyate' iti
atideśaṃ ca asya amunā rūpādiṣu karoti 'tasyaitasya tadeva rūpaṃ yadamuṣya rūpaṃ yāvamuṣya geṣṇau tau geṣṇau yannāma tannāma' iti
sāvadhikaṃ ca īśvaratvamubhayorvyapadiśati'ye cāmuṣmātparāñco loHDsū tṛtīyo'dhyāyaḥ 
kāsteṣāṃ ceṣṭe devakāmānāṃ ca' ityekasya ye caitasmāda rvāñco lokāsteṣāṃ ceṣṭe manuṣyakāmānāṃ ca 'ityekasya yathā idaṃ māgadhasya rājyama rājyama idaṃ vaidehasyeti 
evametebhya setvādivyapadeśebhyo brahmaṇaḥ paramastīti 
evaṃ prāpte pratipādyatemāmānyāntu 
tuśabdena pradarśitāṃ prāptiṃ niruṇaddhi 
na brahmaṇo'nyat kiṃcidbhavitumahīte pramāṇābhāvātna hyanyasyāstitve kiṃcitpramāṇamupalabhāmahe
sarvasya hi janimato vastujātasya janmādi brahmaṇo bhavatīti nirdhāritam ananyatvaṃ ca kāraṇāta kāryasya 
na ca brahmavyatiriktaṃ kiṃcita ajaṃ saṃbhavati 'sadeva somyedamagra āsīdekamevādvitīyama 'ityavadhāraṇāt
ekavijñānena ca sarvavijñānapratijñānāt na brahmavyatiriktavastvastitvamavakalpate 
nanu setvādivyapadeśāḥ brahmavyatiriktaṃ tattvaṃ sūcayantītyuktam 
netyucyate setuvyapadeśastāvat na brahmaṇo bāhyasya sadbhāvaṃ pratipādayituṃ kṣamate
seturātmeti hi āha na ataḥ paramastīti
tatra parasmin asati setutvaṃ nāvakalpata iti paraṃ kimapi kalpyeta
na caitat nyāyyama 
haṭho hi aprasiddhakalpanā s W  sūtrabhāṣye pā api ca setuvyapadeśādātmano laukikasetunidarśanena sabāhyavastutāṃ prasañjayatā mṛhārumayatāpi prāsaṅkhyata
na caitannyāyyam ajatvādiśrutivirodhāt
setusāmānyāttu setuśavda ātmani prayukta iti ṣyate
jagatastanmaryādānāṃ ca vidhārakatvaṃ setusāmānyamātmanaḥ

buddhayartha pāvat 
yadapyuktam unmānavyapadeśādasti paramiti tatrābhidhīyateunmānavyapadeśo'pi na brahmavyatiriktavastvastitvapratipattyarthaḥ
kimarthastarhi  buddhayartha upāsanārtha iti yāvat 
catuṣpādaṣṭāśaphaṃ ṣoḍaśakalamityevaṃrūpābuddhiḥ kathaṃ nu nāma brahmaṇi sthirā syāditi  vikāradvāreṇa brahmaṇa unmānakalpanaiva kriyate 
na hi avikāre'nante brahmaṇi sarvaiḥ puṃbhiḥ śakyā buddhiḥ sthāpayitum mandamadhyamottamabuddhitvāt puṃsāmiti 
pādavat  yathā manaākāśayoradhyātmamadhidaivataṃ ca brahmapratīkayorāmnātayoḥ catvāro vāgādayo mana saṃbandhinaḥ pādāḥ kalpyante catvāraśca agnyādaya āmichhasū tṛtīyo'dhyāyaḥ 
kāśasaṃbandhinaādhyānāya tadvat 
athavā pādavaditi yathā kārṣāpaṇe pādavibhāgo vyavahāraprācuryāya kalpyate na hi sakalenaiva kārṣāpaṇena sarvadā sarve janā vyavahartumīśate krayavikraye parimāṇāniyamāt tadvadityarthaḥ 
MALIZAND sthānaviśeṣātprakāśādivat 
iha sūtre dvayorapi saṃbandhabhedavyapadeśayoḥ parihāro'bhidhīyate 
yadapyuktamsaṃbandhavyapadeśāt bhedavyapadeśāca paramata syāditi tadapyasat
yata ekasyāpi sthānaviśeṣāpekṣayā etau vyapadeśāvupapadyete 
saṃbandhavyapadeśe tāvadayamartha buddhayāyupādhisthānaviśeṣayogādudbhūtasya viśeṣavijñānasya upādhyupaśame ya upaśama sa paramātmanā saṃbandha ityupādhyapekṣayā upacaryate na parimitatvāpekṣayā 
tathā bhedavyapadeśo'pi brahmaṇa upādhibhedāpekṣayaiva upacaryate na svarūpabhedāpekṣayā 
prakāśādivaditi upamopādānam yathā ekasya prakāśasya sauryasya cāndramasasya vā upādhiyogādrupajātaviśeṣasya upādhyupaśamātsaṃbandhavyapadeśo bhavati upādhibhedācca bhedavyapadeśa
yathā vā sūcīpāśākāśādiṣūpādhyapekṣayaivaitau saṃbandhabhedavyapadeśau bhavataḥ tadvat 
upapatteśca sūtrabhāṣye pā ves upapadyate ca atra īdṛśa eva saṃbandha nānyādṛśaḥ 'svamapīto bhavati' iti hi svarūpasaṃbandhamenamāmananti
svarūpasya ca anapāyitvāt na naranagaranyāyena saṃbandho ghaṭate
upādhikṛtasvarūpatirobhāvāttu 'svamapīto bhavati' ityupapadyate 
tathā bhedo'pi nānyādṛśaḥ saṃbhavati bahutaraśrutiprasiddhaikeśvaratvavirodhāt 
tathā ca śrutirekasyāpyākāśamya sthānakṛtaṃ bhedavyapadeśamupapādayati'yo'yaṃ bahirdhā puruṣādākāśa yo'yamantaḥ puruṣa ākāśa yo'yamantahṛdaya ākāśa 'iti 
tathānyapratiṣedhāt 
evaṃ setvādivyapadeśān parapakṣahetūnunmathya saṃprati svapakṣaṃ hetvantareṇopasaṃharati 
tathānyapratiṣedhādapi na brahmaṇaḥ paraṃ vastvantaramastīti gamyate
tathā hi  'sa evādhastāt ahamevādhastāt' ātmaivādhastāt sarve taṃ parādādyo'nyatrātmana sarve veda' 'brahmaivedaṃ sarvam ' 'ātmaivedaṃ sarvam 'neha nānāsti kiṃcana' 'yasmātparaṃ nāparamasti kiṃcit tadetadbrahmāpūrvamanaparamanantaramabāhyam' ityevamādīni vākyāni svaprakaraṇasthāni anyārthatvena pariṇetumaśakyāni brahmavyatiriktaṃ vastvantaraṃ vārayanti 
sarvāntaraśruteścana parasū tṛtīyo'dhyāyaḥ 
mātmano'nyaḥ antarātmā astītyavagamyate 
anena sarvagatatvamāyāmaśabdādibhyaḥ 
anena setvādivyapadeśanirākaraṇena anyapratiṣedhasamāśrayaṇena ca sarvagatatvamapyātmanaḥ siddhaṃ bhavati
anyathā hi tanna sidhyet 
setvādivyapadeśeṣu hi mukhyeṣvaṅgīkriyamāṇeṣu pariccheda ātmana prasajyeta setvādīnāmevamātmakatvāt 
tathā anyapratiṣedhe'pyasati vastu vastvantarāvyāvartata iti pariccheda eva ātmanaḥ prasajyeta 
sarvagatatvaṃ ca asya āyāmaśabdādibhyo'vagamyate
āyāmaśabda vyātivacana śabda 
yāvānvā ayamākāśastāvāneṣo'ntahṛdaya ākāśa ākāśavatsarvagataśca nityaḥ' 'jyāyāndivaḥ 'jyāyānākāśāt nityaḥ sarvagataḥ sthāṇuracalo'yaṃ sanātanaḥ' ityevamādayo hi śrutismṛtinyāyāḥ sarvagatatvamātmano'vabodhayanti 
phalamata upapatteḥ 
tasyaiva brahmaṇo vyāvahārikyām īśitrīśitavyavibhāgāvasthāyām ayamanyaḥ svabhāvāṃ varṇyate 
yadetat iṣṭāniṣṭa vyāmiśralakṣaṇaṃ karmaphalaṃ saṃsāragocaraṃ trividhaṃ prasiddhaṃ jantūnām kimetat karmaṇo phalādhikaraṇam  sūtrabhāṣye pā bhavati āhosvidīśvarāditi bhavati vicāraṇā 
tatra tāva tpratipādyate phalam ataḥ īśvarāt bhavitumarhati 
kuta  upapatte 
sa hi sarvādhyakṣaḥ sṛṣṭisthitisaṃhārān vicitrāna vi dadhat deśakālaviśeṣābhijñatvāt karmiṇāṃ karmānurūpaṃ phalaṃ saṃpādayatītyupapadyate
karmaṇastu anukṣaṇavināśinaḥ kālāntarabhāvi phalaṃ bhavatītyanupapannam abhāvādbhāvānutpatteḥ 
syādetatkarma vinaśyat svakālameva svānurūpaṃ phalaṃ janayitvā vinaśyati tatphalaṃ kālāntaritaṃ kartrā bhokṣyata iti
tadapi na pariśudhyati prāgbhoktṛsaṃbandhāt phalatvānupapatteyatkālaṃ hi yat sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ vā ātmanā bhujyate tasyaiva loke phalatvaṃ prasiddham
na hi asaṃbaddhasyātmanā sukhasya duḥkhasya vā phalatvaṃ pratiyanti laukikāḥ 
atho cyeta mā bhūtkarmānantaraṃ phalotpādaḥ karmakāryādapūrvātphalamutpatsyata iti tadapi nopapadyate apūrvasyācetanasya kāṣṭhaloṣṭasamasya cetanenāpravartitasya pravṛ tyanupapatte tadastitve eva pramāṇābhāvāt 
arthāpattiḥ pramāṇamiti cet na īśvarasiddherarthāpattikṣayāt 
śrutatvāca 
na kevalam upapattereva īśvaraṃ phalahetuṃ kalpayāma kiṃ tarhi śrutatvādapi īśvarameva phalahetuṃ manyāmahe tathā ca śrutirbhavatisū tṛtīyo'dhyāyaḥ 
sa vā eṣa mahānaja ātmānnādo vasudāna' ityevaṃjātīyakā 
dharma jaiminirata eva 
jaiministvācāryo dharma phalasya dātāraṃ manyate ata eva hetoḥ  śruteḥ upapatteśca 
śrūyate tāvadayamartha 'svargakāmo yajeta' ityevamādiṣu vākyeṣu 
tatra ca vidhiśruterviṣa yabhāvopagamāt yāga svargasyotpādaka iti gamyate
anyathā hi ananuṣṭhātṛko yāga āpadyeta
tatra asya upadeśavaiyayai syāt 
nanu anukṣaṇavināśinaḥ karmaṇa phalaṃ nopapadyata iti parityakto'yaṃ pakṣa 
naiṣa doṣaḥ śrutiprāmāṇyāt  śrutiścet pramāṇama yathāyaṃ karmaphalasaṃbandhaḥ śruta upapadyate tathā kalpayitavyaḥ 
na ca anutpādya kimadhyapūrva karma vinaśyat kālāntaritaṃ phalaṃ dātuṃ śaknoti
ataḥ karmaṇo vā sūkṣmā kāciduttarāvasthā phalasya vā pūrvāvasthā apūrva nāma astīti tarjyate 
upapadyate ca ayamartha uktena prakāreṇa 
īśvarastu phalaṃ dadātītyanupapannam avicitrasya kāraṇasya vicitlakāryānupapatteḥ vaiṣamyanairghṛṇyaprasaṅgāt tadnuṣṭhānavaiyarthyāpatteśca 
tasmāt dharmādeva phalamiti 
pūrva tu bādarāyaṇo hetuvyapadeśāt sūtrabhāṣye pā bādarāyaṇastvācārya pūrvoktameva īśvaraṃ phalahetuṃ manyate 
kevalātkarmaṇa apūrvādvā kevalāna phalamityayaṃ pakṣa tuśabdena vyāvartyate 
karmāpekṣāta apūrvāpekṣādvā yathā tathāstu īśvarātphalamiti siddhānta 
kuta  hetuvyapadeśāt
dharmādharmayorapi hi kārayitṛtvena īśvaro hetuḥ vyapadiśyate phalasya ca dātṛtvena eṣa hyeva sādhu karma kārayati taṃ yamebhyo lokebhya unninīṣate 
eṣa u evāsādhu karma kārayati taṃ yamadho ninīpate' iti 
smaryate ca ayamartho bhagaE vadgītāsu  'yo yo yāṃ yāṃ tanuṃ bhaktaḥ śraddhayācitumicchati 
tasya tasyācalāṃ śraddhāṃ tāmeva vidadhāmyaham 
sa tayā śraddhayā yuktastasyārādhanamahate 
labhate ca tataḥ kāmān mayaiva vihitānhitān' iti 
sarvavedānteṣu ca īśvarahetukā eva sṛṣṭayo vyapadiśyante 
tadeva ca īśvarasya phalahetutvama yat svakarmānurūpā prajā sṛjati 
vicitrakāryānupapattyādayo'pi doṣāḥ kṛtaprayatnāpekṣatvādīśvarasya na prasajyante

brahmasūtrabhāṣyam 
tṛtīyādhyāye tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥtṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ 
vyākhyātaṃ vijñeyasya brahmaṇaḥ tattvam
idānīṃ tu prativedāntaṃ vijñānāni bhidyante na veti vicāryate 
nanu vijñeyaṃ brahma pūrvāparādibhedarahitam ekarasaṃ saindhavaghanavat avadhāritam 
tatra kuto vijñānabhedābhedacintāvasara  na hi karmabahutvavat brahmabahutvamapi vedānteṣu pratipipādayiṣitamiti śakyaṃ vaktum brahmaṇa ekatvāt ekarūpatvācca 
na ca ekarūpe brahmaṇi anekarūpāṇi vijñānāni saṃbhavanti
na hi anyathā artha anyathā jñānamityabhrāntaṃ bhavati
yadi puna ekasminbrahmaṇi bahūni vijñānāni vedānteṣu pratipipādayiṣitāni teṣām ekamabhrāntam bhrāntāni itarāṇīti anāśvāsaprasaṅgo vedānteṣu 
tasmānna tāvatprativedāntaṃ brahmavijñānabheda āśaṅkituṃ śakyate 
nāpyasya codanādyaviśeṣādabheda ucyeta brahmavijñānasya acodanālakṣaṇatvāt 
avidhipradhānairha vastuparyavasāyibhi brahmavākyaiḥ mit sūtrabhāṣye pā brahmavijñānaṃ janyata ityavocadācārya 'tattu samanvayāt' ityatra 
tatkathamimāṃ bhedābheda cintāmārabhata iti 
taducyate saguṇabrahmaviṣayā prāṇādiviṣayā ca iyaṃ vijñānabhedābhedacintetyadoṣaḥ 
atra hi karmavat upāsanānāṃ bhedābhedau saṃbhavataḥ
karmavadeva ca upāsanāni dṛṣṭaphalāni aṣṭaphalāni ca ucyante kramamuktiphalāni ca kānicit samyagdarśanotpattidvāreṇa 
teṣu eṣā cintā saṃbhavati kiṃ prativedāntaṃ vijñānabhedaḥ āhosvit neti 
tatra pūrvapakṣahetavastāvadupanyasyante nāmnastāvat bhedapratipattihetutvaṃ prasiddhaṃ jyotirādiṣu 
asti ca atra vedāntāntaravihiteṣu vijñāneṣu anyadanyat nāmataittirīyakaṃ vājasaneyakaṃ kauthumakaṃ kauṣītakaṃ śāṭyāyanakamityevamādi 
tathā rūpabhedo'pi karmabhedasya pratipādaka prasiddhaḥ 'vaiśvadevyāmikṣā vājibhyo vājinam' ityevamādiṣu
asti ca atra rūpabheda 
tadyathākecicchākhina pañcāgnividyāyāṃ ṣaṣṭhamaparamagnimāmananti apare punaḥ pañcaiva paṭhanti
tathā prāṇasaṃvādādiṣu kecit ūnānvāgādīnāmananti kecidadhikān 
tathā dharmaviśeṣo'pi karmabhedasya pratipādaka āśakita kārīryādiṣu 
asti ca atra dharmaviśeṣa 
yathā āthaMAR sū tṛtīyo'dhyāyaḥ 
rvaṇikānāṃ śirovratamiti 
evaṃ punaruktyādayo'pi bhedahetavaḥ yathāsaṃbhavaṃ vedāntāntareṣu yojayitavyāḥ 
tasmāt prativedāntaṃ vijñānabheda ityevaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ sarvavedāntapratyayaṃ codanādyaviśeṣāt 
karaṇam 
sarvavedāntapratyayāni vijñānāni tasmin tasmina vedānte tāni tānyeva bhavitumarhanti 
kuta  codanādyaviśeṣāta 
sarvavedāntaādigrahaṇena śākhāntarādhikaraṇasiddhāntapratyayādhisūtroditā abhedahetava ihākṛṣyante saṃyogarūpacodanākhyāviśeṣādityarthaḥ 
yathā ekamninnagnihotre śākhābhede'pi puruṣaprayatnastādṛśa eva codyatejuhuyāditi evama 'yo ha vai jyeṣṭhaṃ ca śreṣṭhaṃ ca veda' iti vājasaneyināṃ chandogānāṃ ca tādṛśyeva codanā 
prayojanasaṃyogo'pyaviśiṣṭa eva 'jyeṣṭhaśca śreṣṭhaśca svānāṃ bhavati' iti 
rūpamapyubhayatra tadeva vijñānasya yaduta jyeṣṭha śreṣṭhādiviśeṣaṇānvitaṃ prāṇatattvamyathā ca dravyadevate yāgasya rūpama evaṃ vijñeyaṃ rūpaṃ vijñānasya 
tena hi tat rūpyate 
samākhyāpi saivaprāṇavidyeti 
tasmāt sarvavedāntapratyayatvaṃ vijñānānām 
evaṃ pañcāgnividyā vaiśvānaravidyā śāṇḍilyavidyetyevamādiṣvapi yojayitavyam 
ye tu nāmarūpādayo bhedahesūtrabhāṣye pā tvābhāsāḥ te prathama eva kāṇḍe 'na nāmnā syādacodanābhidhānatvāt' ityārabhya parihṛtāḥ 
ihāpi kaṃcidviśeṣamāśaṅkaya pariharati bhedānneti cennaikayāmapi 
syādetat sarvavedāntapratyayatvaṃ vijñānānāṃ guṇabhedāt nopapadyate
tathā hi  vājasaneyinaḥ pañcāgnividyāṃ prastutya ṣaṣṭhamaparamagnimāmananti'tasyāgnirevāgnirbhavati' ityādinā 
chandogāstu taṃ na āmananti pañcasaṃkhyayaiva ca te upasaṃharanti 'atha ha ya etānevaṃ pañcāgnīnveda' iti 
yeṣāṃ ca sa guṇo'sti yeṣāṃ ca nāsti kathamubhayeṣāmekā vidyopapadyeta  na ca atra guṇopasaṃhāra śakyate pratyetuma pañcasaṃkhyāvirodhāt

kathaṃ hi iha ekaviṃśatā ādityasyābhidhīyeta anapekṣyamāṇe'rthavādāntare 'dvādaśa māsā sūtrabhāṣye pā pañcartavastraya ime lokā asāvāditya ekaviṃśaḥ' ityasmina  tathā 'triṣṭubhau bhavataḥ sendriyatvāya' ityevamādivādeṣu 'indriyaṃ vai triṣṭup' ityevamādyarthavādāntarāpekṣā dṛśyate 
vidyāstutya rthatvācca asyopāyanavādasya kathamanyadīye sukṛtaduṣkṛte anyairupeyete iti nātīvābhiniveṣṭavyam 
upāyanaśabda śeṣatvāditi ca śabdaśabdaṃ samuccārayan stutyarthāmeva hānāvupāyanānuvṛttiṃ sūcayati
guṇopasaṃhāravivakṣāyāṃ hi upāyanārthasyaiva hānāvanuvṛtti brūyāt 
tasmāt guṇopasaṃhāravicāraprasaṅgena stutyupasaṃhārapradarśanārthamidaṃ sūtram 
kuśācchandastutyupagānabaditi upamobhāllavinām 'kuśā vānaspatyā stha tā mā pāta' ityetasminnigame kuśānāmaviśeṣeṇa vanaspatiyonitvaśravaṇe śāṭyāyanināma 'audumbarāḥ' iti viśeṣavacanāt audumbarya kuśā āśrīyante
yathā ca kvacit devāsuracchandasāmaviśeṣeṇa paurvāparyaprasaṅge devacchandāṃsi pūrvāṇīti paiṅgayāmnānātpratīyate
yathā ca ṣoḍaśistotre keṣāṃ citkālāviśeṣaprāptau 'samayādhyuṣite sūrye' ityārcaśruteḥ kālaviśeṣapratipatti 
yathaiva ca aviśeṣeṇopagānaṃ keci tsamāmananti viśeṣeṇa bhālavina yathā eteṣu kuśādiṣu śrutyantaragataviśeṣānvayaḥ evaṃ hānāvapyupāyanānvaya ityarthaḥ 
pādānam
tadyathāsū tṛtīyo'dhyāyaḥ 
FOR śrutyantarakṛtaṃ hi viśeṣaṃ śrutyantare'nabhyupagacchataḥ sarvatraiva vikalpa syāt 
sa ca anyāyyaḥ satyāṃ gatau
taduktaṃ dvādaśalakṣaṇyām'api tu vākyaśeṣatvāditaraparyudāsaḥ syātpratiṣedhe vikalpa syāt' iti 
athavā etāsveva vidhūnanaśrutiṣu etena sūtreṇa etañcinta yitavyam kimanena vidhūnanavacanena sukṛtaduṣkṛtayonamabhidhīyate kiṃ vā arthāntaramiti 
tatra ca evaṃ prāpayitavyam na hānaṃ vidhūnanamabhidhīyate 'dhūkampane' iti smaraṇāt dodhūyante dhvajāgrāṇi 'iti ca vāyunā cālyamāneṣu dhvajāgreṣu prayogadarśanāt
tasmāt cālanaṃ vidhūnanamabhidhīyate
cālanaṃ tu sukṛtaduṣkṛtayo kaṃcitkālaṃ phalapratibandhanātityevaṃ prāpayya prativaktavyam hānāveva eṣa vidhūnanaśabdo vartitumarhati upāyanaśabdaśeṣatvāt 
na hi paraparigrahabhūtayoḥ sukṛtaduṣkṛtayo aprahīṇayo parairupāyanaṃ saṃbhavati 
yadyapi idaṃ parakīyayoḥ sukṛtaduṣkṛtayo parairupāyanaṃ na āñjasaṃ saṃbhāvyate tathāpi tatsaṃkīrtanāttāvat tadānuguṇyena hānameva vidhūnanaṃ nāmeti nirṇetuṃ śakyate 
kvacidapi ca idaṃ vidhūnanasaṃnidhāvupāyanaṃ śrayamāṇaṃ kuśācchandastutyupagānavat vidhūnanaśrutyā sarvatrāpekṣyamāṇaṃ sārvatrikaṃ nirṇayasūtrabhāṣye pā kāraṇaṃ saṃpadyate 
na ca cālanaṃ dhvajāgravat sukṛtaduṣkṛtayormukhyaṃ saṃbhavati adravyatvāt 
aśvaśca romāṇi vidhūnvāna tyajana raja sahaiva tena romāṇyapi jīrṇāni śātayati  'aśva iva romāṇi vidhūya pāpama' iti ca brāhmaṇama
anekārthatvābhyupagamācca dhātūnāṃ na smaraṇavirodha 
taduktamiti vyākhyātam 
sāṃparāye tartavyābhāvāttathā hyanye 
devayānena pathā paryaṅkasthaṃ brahma abhiprasthitasya vyadhvani sukṛtaduṣkṛtayorviyogaṃ kauṣītakina paryaṅkavidyāyāmāmananti sāṃparāyā' sa etaṃ devayānaṃ panthānamāsādyāgnidhikaraṇam 
lokamāgacchati' ityupakramya 'sa āgacchati virajāṃ nadīṃ tāṃ manasaivātyeti tatsukṛtaduṣkṛte vidhūnute' iti 
tat kiṃ yathā śrutaṃ vyadhvanyeva viyogavacanaṃ pratipattavyam āhosvit ādāveva dehādapasarpaṇe iti vicāra ṇāyām śrutiprāmāṇyāt yathā śruti pratipattiprasaktau paṭhati sāṃparāya iti 
sāṃparāye gamana eva dehādapasarpaṇe idaṃ vidyāsāmarthyātsukṛtaduṣkṛtahānaṃ bhavati iti pratijānīte
hetuṃ ca ācaṣṭe tartavyābhāvāditi 
na hi viduṣaḥ saṃparetasya vidyayā brahma saṃprepsata antarāle sukṛtaduṣkṛtābhyāṃ kiṃsū tṛtīyo'dhyāyaḥ 
citprāptavyamasti yadarthe katicitkṣaṇānakṣīṇe te kalpeyātām 
vidyāviruddhaphalatvācca vidyāsāmarthyena tayoḥ kṣaya 
sa ca yadaiva vidyā phalābhimukhī tadaiva bhavitumarhati 
tasmāt prāgeva san ayaṃ sukṛtaduṣkṛtakṣayaḥ paścātpaṭhyate 
tathā hi a nye'pi śākhina tāṇḍina śāṭyāyaninaśca prāgavasthāyāmeva sukṛtaduṣkṛtahānamāmananti  'ava iva romāṇi vidhūya pāpam' iti 'tasya putrā dāyamupayanti suhṛdaḥ sādhukṛtyāṃ dviṣanta pāpakṛtyām' iti ca 
chandata ubhayāvirodhāt 
yadi ca dehādapasṛptasya devayānena pathā prasthitasya ardhapathe sukṛtaduṣkṛtakṣayo'bhyupagamyeta tataḥ patite dehe yamaniyamavidyābhyāsātmakasya sukṛtaduṣkṛtakṣayahetoḥ puruṣayatnasya icchāto'nuṣṭhānānupapatte anupapattireva taddhetukasya sukṛtaduṣkṛtakṣayasya syāt
tasmāt pūrvameva sādhakāvasthāyāṃ chandato'nuṣṭhānaṃ tasya syāt tatpūrvakaṃ ca sukṛtaduṣkṛtahānam iti draṣṭavyam
evaṃ nimittanaimittika yorupapattiḥ tāṇḍiśāṭyāyaniśrutyośca saṃgatiriti 
gaterarthavattvamubhayathānyathā hi virodhaḥ 
sūtrabhāṣye pā kvacit puṇyapāpāpahānasaṃnidhau devayānaḥ panthāḥ śrūyate kacinna
tatra saṃśayaḥ kiṃ hānāvaviśeṣeṇaiva devayāna gaterarthapanthā saṃnipateta uta vibhāgena kvacitsaṃvattvādhinipatet kvacinneti 
yathā tāvat hānāvakaraṇam 
viśeṣeṇaiva upāyanānuvṛttiruktā evaṃ devayānānuvṛttirapi bhavitumarhatītyasyāṃ prāptau ācakṣmahegate devayānasya patha arthavattvam ubhayathā vibhāgena bhavitumarhati kvacidarthavatī gatiḥ kacinnati 
na aviśeṣeṇa 
anyathā hi aviśeṣeṇaiva etasyāṃ gatāvaṅgīkriyamāṇāyāṃ virodhaḥ syāt 'puṇyapāpe vidhūya nirañjanaḥ paramaṃ sāmyamupaiti' ityasyāṃ śrutau deśāntaraprāpaṇī gativirudhyeta
kathaṃ hi nirajano'gantā deśāntaraṃ gacchet
gantavyaṃ ca paramaṃ sāmyaṃ na deśāntaraprāptyāyattamityānarthakyamevātra gatermanyāmahe

na tu samyagdarśane tallakṣaṇārthopalabdhirasti

aniyamaḥ sarvāsāmavirodhaḥ śabdānumānābhyām

lavidyāyāṃ pañcāgnividyāyāṃ daharavidyāyāmiti 
na anyāsuyathā madhuvidyāyāṃ śāṇḍilyavidyāyāṃ ṣoḍaśakalavidyāyāṃ vaiśvānaravidyāyāmiti

uta aniyamena sarvābhireva evaṃjātīyakābhirvidyābhirabhisaṃbadhyeteti

nanu aniyamābhyupagame prakaraṇavirodha naiṣo'sti virodha
śabdānumānābhyāṃ śrutismṛtibhyāmityarthaḥ
tathā hi śruti 'tadya itthaṃ viduḥ' iti pañcāgnividyāvatāṃ devayānaṃ panthānamavatārayantī 'ye cemeḍaraṇye śraddhā tapa ityupāsate' iti vidyāntaraśīlināmapi pañcāgnividyāvidbhiḥ samānamārgatāṃ gamayati 
kathaṃ punaravagamyatevidyāntaraśīlināmiyaṃ gatiriti  nanu śraddhātapaparāyaṇānāmeva syāt tanmātraśravaṇāt naiṣa doṣaḥ

na tatra dakṣiṇā yanti nāvidvāṃsastapasvinaḥ' iti śrutyanta sū tṛtīyo'dhyāyaḥ

ata uttaramucyate na teṣām apāntaratamaḥ prabhṛtīnāṃ ve dapravartanādiṣu lokasthitihetuṣvadhikāreṣu niyuktānām adhikāratantratvātsthiteḥ 
yathāsau bhagavānsavitā sahasrayugaparya ntaṃ jagato'dhikāraṃ caritvā tadavasāne udayāstamayavarjitaṃ kaivalyamanubhavati 'atha tata ūrdhva udetya naivodetā nāstametaikala eva madhye sthātā' iti śrute

sakṛtpravṛttameva hi te phaladānāya karmāśayamativāhayantaḥ svātantryeṇaiva gṛhādiva gṛhāntaram anyamanyaṃ dehaṃ saṃcaranta svādhikāranirvartanāya aparimuṣitasmṛtaya eva dehendriyaprakṛtivaśitvāt nirmāya dehān yugapat krameṇa vā adhitiṣṭhanti

prastāvādidevatāvijñāna vihīnānāmapi prastotrādīnāṃ yājanādhyavasānadarśanātū 'prastotaryā devatā prastāvamanvāyattā tāṃ cedavidvānprastoṣyasi ' 'tāṃ cedavidvānugāmyasi 'tāṃ cedavidvānpratihariṣyasi 'iti ca 
api ca evaṃjātīyakasya karmavyapāśrayasya vijñānasya pṛthageva karmaṇa phalama upalabhyatekarmaphalasiddhyapratibandhaḥ tatsamṛddhi atiśayaviśeṣa kaścit 'tenobhau kuruto yaścaitadevaṃ veda yaśca na veda 
nānā tu vidyā cāvidyā ca yadeva vidyayā karoti śraddhayopaniṣadā tadeva vīryavattaraṃ bhavati' iti
tatra 'nānā tu 'iti vidvadavidvatprayogayo pṛthakkaraṇāta 'vīryavattaram' iti ca tara pratyayaprayogān vidyāhīnamapi vīryavaditi gamyate
tacca anityatve vidyāyā upapadyate 
nityatve tu kathaṃ tadvihīnaṃ karma vīryavadityanujñāyeta
sarvāṅgopasaṃhāre hi vīryava tkarmeti sthitiḥ 
tathā lokasāmādiṣu pratiniyatāni pratyupāsanaṃ phalāni śiṣyante 'kalpate hāsmai lokā ūrdhvā śrāvṛttā' ityevamādīni 
na cedaṃ phalaśravaṇama arthavādamātraṃ yuktaṃ pratipattum 
tathā hi guṇavāda āpadyeta
phalopadeśe tu mukhyavādopapatti prayājādiṣu tu itikartavyatākāṅkṣasya kato sū tṛtīyo'dhyāyaḥ 
prakṛtatvāt tāda sati yuktaṃ phalaśruterarthavādatvam 
tathā anārabhyādhīteṣvapi parṇamayītvādiṣu na hi parṇamayītvādīnāmakriyātmakānām āśrayamantareṇa phalasaṃbandho'vakalpate 
godohanādīnāṃ hi prakṛtāppraṇayanādyāśrayalābhādupapanna phalavidhi
tathā bailvādīnāmapi prakṛtayūpādyāśraya lābhādupapannaḥ phalavidhi 
na tu parṇamayītvādiṣu evaṃvidhaḥ kaścidāśrayaḥ prakṛto'sti
vākyenaiva tu juhvādyāśrayatāṃ vivakṣitvā phale'pi vidhiṃ vivakṣato vākyabheda syāt 
upāsanānāṃ tu kriyātmakatvāt viśiṣṭavidhānopapatteḥ udgīthādyāśrayāṇāṃ phale vidhānaṃ na virudhyate 
tasmāt yathā ṛtvāśrayāṇyapi godohanādīni phalasaṃyogādanityāni evamudgīthādyupāsanānyapi iti draṣṭavyam 
ata eva ca kalpasūtrakārā naivaṃjātīyakānyupāsanāni ṛtuṣu kalpayāṃcakruḥ 
pradānavadeva taduktam 
vājasaneyake 'vadiṣyāmyevāhamiti vāgdadhre' ityatra adhyātmaṃ vāgādīnāṃ prāṇaḥ śreṣṭho'vadhāritaḥ adhidaivatamagnyādīnāṃ vāyuḥ
tathā chāndogye 'vāyurvāva dhikaraṇam 
saṃvarga 'ityatra adhidaivatam agnyādīnāṃ vāyu saṃvargo'vadhāritaḥ prāṇo vāva saṃvarga' ityatra pradānāS W sūtrabhāṣye pā adhyātmaṃ vāgādīnāṃ prāṇaḥ 
tatra saṃśayakiṃ pṛthagevemau vāyuprāṇāvupagantavyau syātām uta apṛthagiti 
apṛthagiti tāvatprāptam tattvābhedāt
na hi abhinne tattve pṛthaganucintanaṃ nyāyyama 
darśayati ca śrutiḥ adhyātmamadhidaivataṃ ca tattvābhedam 'agnirvāgbhūtvā mukhaṃ prāviśat' ityārabhya
tathā 'ta ete sarva eva samāḥ sarve'nantāḥ' iti ādhyātmikānāṃ prāṇānām ādhidaivika vi bhūtimātmabhūtāṃ darśayati 
tathā anyatrāpi tatra tatra adhyātmamadhidaivataṃ ca bahudhā tattvābhedadarśanaṃ bhavati 
kacicca 'ya prāṇaḥ sa vāyu 'iti spaṣṭameva vāyuṃ prāṇaṃ ca ekaṃ karoti 
tathā udāhṛte'pi vājasaneyibrāhmaṇe 'yatacodeti sūrya 'ityasmin upasaṃhāraloke 'prāṇādvā eṣa udeti prāṇe'stameti' iti prāṇenaiva upasaṃharan ekatvaṃ darśayati
'tasmādekameva vrataṃ caretprāṇyāñcaivāpānyācca 'iti ca prāṇavratenaiva ekenopasaṃharan etadeva draḍhayati 
tathā chāndogye'pi parastāta 'mahātmanaścaturo deva ekaḥ kaḥ sa jagāra bhuvanasya gopā 'ityekameva saṃvarga gamayati
na bravīti eka eva eṣāṃ caturṇāṃ saṃvarga aparo'pareṣāmiti

brūmaḥ pṛthageva vāyuprāṇāvupagantavyāviti
kasmāt  pṛthagupadeśāt
ādhyānārtho hi ayam adhyātmādhidaivavibhāgopadeśaḥ
saḥ asatyādhyānapṛthaktve anarthaka eva syāt 
nanu uktam apṛthaganucintanaṃ tattvābhedāditi naiṣa doṣaḥ
tattvābhede'pyavasthābhedāt upadeśabhedavaśena anucintanabhedopapatte lokopanyāsasya ca tattvābhedābhiprāyeṇāpi upapadyamānasya pūrvodita dhyeyabhedanirākaraṇasāmarthyābhāvāt 'sa yathaiṣāṃ prāṇānāṃ madhyamaḥ prāṇa evametāsāṃ devatānāṃ vāyuḥ' iti ca upamānopameyakaraṇāt 
etena vratopanyāso vyākhyāta 
'ekameva vratam' iti ca evakāraḥ vāgādidvratanivartanena prāṇavratapratipattyartha
bhagnavratāni hi vāgādīnyuktāni tāni mṛtyuḥ śramo bhūtvopayeme' iti śruteḥ 
na vāyuvratanivṛttyarthaḥ 'athāto vratamīmāṃsā' iti prastutya tulyavat vāyuprāṇayorabhagnavratatvasya nirdhāritatvāt 
'ekameva vrataṃ caret' iti ca uktvā 'teno etasyai devatāyai sāyujyaṃ salokatāṃ jayati' iti vāyuprāptiṃ phalaṃ bruvan vāyuvratamanivartitaṃ māyane yati
devatetyatra vāyu syāt aparicchinnātmakatvasya propsatatvāt purastātprayogācca 'saiṣānastamitā devatā ya sūtrabhāṣye pā dvāyu 'iti 
tathā 'tau vā etau dvau saṃvargo vāyureva deveṣu prāṇaḥ prāṇeṣu' iti bhedena vyapadiśati
'te vā ete pañcānye pañcānye daśa santastatkṛtam' iti ca bhedenaiva upasaṃharati

COMI pūrvavikalpaḥ prakaraṇātsyātkriyā mānasavat

E nanu liṅgamapi asatyāmanyasyāṃ prāptau asādhakaṃ kasyacidarthasyeti apāsya tat prakaraṇasāmarthyāt kriyāśeṣatvamadhyavasitamityata uttaraṃ paṭhati śrutyādibalīyastvācca na bādhaḥ 
naivaṃ prakaraṇasāmarthyātkriyāśeṣatvamadhyavasāya svātantryapakṣo bādhitavya śrutyāderbalīyastvāt

tāni ca iha svātantryapakṣaṃ sādhayanti dṛśyante
katham  śruti stāvat  'te haite vidyācita eva' iti
tathā liṅgama' sarvadā sarvāṇi bhūtāni cinvantyapi svapate' iti
tathā vākyamapi 'vidyayā haivaita evaṃvidaścitā bhavanti' iti  sūtrabhāṣye pā 'vidyācita eva' iti hi sāvadhāraṇā iyaṃ śrutiḥ kriyānupraveśe'mīṣāmabhyupagamyamāne pīḍitā syāt 
nanu abāhyasādhanatvābhiprāyamidamavadhāraṇaṃ bhaviṣyati netyucyate 
ta dabhiprāyatāyāṃ hi 'vidyācita 'iti iyatā svarūpasaṃkīrtanenaiva kṛtatvāt anarthakamavadhāraṇaṃ bhavet svarūpameva hi eṣām abāhyasādhanatvamiti
abāhyasādhanatve'pi tu mānasaprahavat kriyānupraveśaśaṅkāyāṃ tannivṛttiphalam avadhāraṇama arthavadbhaviyati

karṇābhyāṃ bhūri viśruvam 
brahmaṇaḥ kośo'si medhayā pihitaḥ 
śrutaṃ me gopāya 
oṃ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ 
ahaṃ vṛkṣasya rekhā 
kīrtiḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ gireriva 
ūrdhvapavitro vājinīva svamṛ tamasmi 
draviṇa savarcasam 
sumedhā amṛtokṣitaḥ 
iti triśaṅkorvedānuvacanam 
oṃ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ 
CSS bhadraṃ karṇebhiḥ śṛṇuyāma devāḥ 
bhadraṃ paśyemākṣabhiryajatrāḥ 
sthirairaṅgaistuṣṭuvā sastanūbhiḥ 
vyaśema devahitaṃ yadāyuḥ 
svasti na indro vṛddhaśravāḥ 
svasti naḥ pūṣā viśvavedāḥ 
svasti na stārkṣyo ariṣṭanemiḥ 
svasti no bṛhaspatirdadhātu 
oṃ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ 
SONpūrṇamadaḥ pūrṇamidaṃ pūrṇātpūrṇamudacya te 
pūrṇasya pūrṇamādāya pūrṇamevāvaśiyate 
oṃ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ 
MLA āpyāyantu mamāṅgāni vākū prāṇaścakṣuḥ śrotramatho balamindriyāṇi ca sarvāṇi 
sarva brahmaupaniṣadaṃ māhaṃ brahma nirākuryāṃ mā mā brahma nirākarodanirākaraṇamastvanirākaraṇaṃ me'stu 
tadātmani nirate ya upaniṣatsu dharmāste mayi santu te mayi santu 
oṃ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ vāṅ me manasi pratiṣṭhitā 
mano me vāci pratiṣṭhitam 
āvirāvīrma edhi 
vedasya ma āṇīsthaḥ 
śrutaṃ me mā prahāsīḥ 
anenādhītena 
ahorātrānsaṃdadhāmi 
ṛtaṃ vadiṣyāmi 
satyaṃ vadiṣyāmi 
tanmāmavatu 
tadvaktāramavatu 
avatu mām 
avatu vaktāramavatu vaktāram 
oṃ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ 
bhadraṃ no'pi vātaya manaḥ 
oṃ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ yo brahmāṇaṃ vidadhāti pūrva yo vai vedāṃśca prahiṇoti tasmai 
ta ha devamātmabuddhiprakāśaṃ mumukṣurve śaraṇamahaṃ prapadye 
oṃ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ sūtrānukramaṇikā
śrīḥ
